Current Commentary: The Reefs of the Roosevelt Administration (Part Two)

— Some Observations

The Roosevelt administration is currently enveloped in an atmosphere of high inflation. From the authorities to the farmers, almost everyone considers lowering the commodity value of currency as the best way to escape the current panic, regardless of the ultimate consequences. In particular, the majority support for inflation policies in both the U.S. Senate and House of Representatives is sufficient to illustrate the future of American monetary policy. It is indeed a noteworthy phenomenon in the recovery movement.

However, I cannot help but wonder if the inflation policy will truly contribute to Roosevelt's prosperity plan. Since taking office, Roosevelt has aimed to salvage the panic every day, such as abandoning the gold standard, convening the London Conference, formulating the National Industrial Recovery Act, revising the banking bill, massively purchasing public bonds, and, most recently, manipulating the domestic and foreign gold markets. The methods can be said to be numerous. However, in terms of its effectiveness, not only has there been no gain, but it has also increasingly plunged the American economy into a state of panic. Reviewing his past political achievements, it is no different from using the economic lives of 120 million people as a large experimental field. The current trend toward direct inflation is probably its final experiment. However, since the day Woodin left office, Wall Street financial capitalists, for the sake of protecting creditor interests, have launched attacks on the government, which are no less than plaintive laments. The resolution of the U.S. Chamber of Commerce on the 18th further confirms this. The promotion of a prosperity plan is supposed to target the entire national economy. Now, the clamor for inflating the currency is high among farmers, and the demonstration movement of financial capitalists has followed. The opposition of social classes is triggered by the shift of benefits caused by inflation. How will this resolve the basic tasks of the recovery movement?

Furthermore, the effect of inflation lies in the upward movement of prices, especially in the development of purchasing power and the elimination of overproduction. Only then can the foundation of prosperity be firmly established. Otherwise, the trial implementation of any policy will only intensify social contradictions and will not save the economic crisis. This can be illustrated by simply observing the facts since Roosevelt took office. According to the various indices published by the Federal Reserve Bank of the United States, which uses the average of 1923 to 1925 as the base, they are specially recorded as follows:

March 1933　July 1933

Manufacturing Production　57.0　10.10

Factory Employment　56.6　70.1

Factory Wages　36.9　49.9

Store Sales　55.0　71.0

Looking at the above figures, from March to July, the increase in manufacturing production reached 77 percent, while the increase in factory wages was only 35 percent. The increase in factory employment was even less than 23 percent. The increase in production has already exceeded the rate of increase in total wages, and the increase in worker employment is even lagging behind the progress of production. The stagnation in store sales further proves the weakness of social purchasing power. If this is the case and the contradiction of overproduction is not eliminated, it is no wonder that the stalemate of the economic panic will ultimately not be broken. With the Roosevelt government's accumulated months of effort, and the resulting effect is only this much. Now, to say that prosperity can be achieved immediately by means of inflation is not something we dare to believe. In yesterday's (18th) speech in Savannah, Roosevelt admitted that the economic chronic illness has lasted for twelve years. To seek a cure so that everyone benefits is not easy and cannot be achieved in a year. This shows that the success of the recovery plan is not easy.

Inside Story of the Fujian Incident

Creating Party and Government Organs by Pretending to Reflect Public Opinion

Alliance with Russia and Tolerance of Communism to Implement Land Revolution

(Nanchang) Chen Mingshu's organization of the Social Democratic Party and attempt to use the power of the 19th Route Army to rebel against the central government had been brewing for a long time and was well known to outsiders. In recent months, Chen has been living in Hong Kong, actively campaigning. On the one hand, he has been trying to win over the Third Party, and on the other hand, he has been using Third Party leaders such as Huang Qixiang to contact the Communist Party and the bandit troops of the Jiangxi-Fujian region to act in concert with him. At the beginning of this month, Chen went to Fujian from Hong Kong, and this conspiracy gradually became apparent. The Central News Agency reporter inquired in detail from the military and political organs and learned the inside story. The gist is recorded as follows: When Chen first arrived in Fujian, Third Party leaders such as Huang Qixiang accompanied him. They immediately held secret meetings and planned to organize the People's Government of the Republic of China in Fujian. Its internal organization was as follows: Li Jishen as chairman, Chen as administrative commissioner, Cai Tingkai as military and political commissioner, and Xu Xiqing as economic commissioner. On the afternoon of the 20th of this month, a citizens' meeting was held in Fuzhou, forcibly violating public opinion to create party and government organs. The Revolutionary Committee was formed by the Third Party and the Social Democratic Party. It is reported that what they are advocating is to implement land revolution, re-adopt the agricultural and industrial policies of the past period of tolerating communism, and say that to save the country today, we must ally with Russia, and to ally with Russia, we must tolerate communism. If the 19th Route Army in Fujian does not ally with the Communists, it will be destroyed by the Communists. As for the flag they planned to adopt, it was half red and half red, yellow, blue, white, and black, all of which were the propositions of the Social Democratic Party and the Third Party. Earlier, when Chen Mingshu was in Hong Kong, Huang Qixiang, Peng Zexiang and others, as representatives, contacted the Communist Party and the Communist bandits of Fujian and Jiangxi separately. Later, on the Communist bandits' side, the wife of Luo Liehui, the false commander-in-chief of the Fujian Military Region, also went to Hong Kong to meet Chen and discussed everything in person. A military agreement of mutual non-aggression has now been reached with the Communist bandits, and it has been agreed that the Fujian side will supply the bandit areas of Jiangxi and Fujian with 300,000 yuan worth of salt, 300,000 yuan worth of medicines, and 100,000 yuan worth of military equipment as a prerequisite for mutual cooperation. The wife of Peng Dehuai, a major Communist bandit leader, and representatives of the Communist bandits are still staying in Fuzhou for further liaison. However, Fujian is close to Taiwan. Once something happens, it is feared that Japan will take advantage of it. Therefore, in recent months, Chen has been working hard to cooperate with Japan. Considering the 19th Route Army's experience in resisting Japan in Shanghai, it could not change its face for a while. It followed Fang Ji's old tricks, still advocating national salvation and resistance to Japan on the one hand, and entrusting Chen Youren, Han Baoli, and others to repeatedly seek understanding from the Taiwan Governor's Office on the other hand. Recently, it was reported that Chen had been assisted with 3 million yuan through Han's agency. Thus, Li Jichun and Fang Zhenwu's comrades are not alone. Analyzing the content of this Fujian incident, it is not simple at all. It is actually using the party to oppose the party, using resistance to Japan to compromise with Japan, and using the suppression of the Communists to cooperate with the Communists. The deception has reached this point. Not only have those who share Chen's political line become suspicious, but even the generals within the 19th Route Army are uneasy. (Central News Agency dispatch, 21st)

Japan's Attitude Toward Fujian: Unwilling to Interfere if There Are No Anti-Japanese Actions

(Tokyo) The Japanese Foreign Ministry has cabled the Japanese Consul General in Fuzhou, stating that if the Fujian independence movement does not adopt an anti-Japanese attitude or endanger the lives and property of Japanese residents, the Japanese government is unwilling to interfere. Authorities subtly indicated that this directive contained the meaning that if the independence movement in Fujian Province adopted an anti-Japanese attitude or endangered the lives and property of Japanese residents, Japan might have to intervene. (Reuters dispatch, 20th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the independence of Fujian, the Foreign Ministry will instruct the Consul General in Fuzhou, Moriya, and Minister Arima with the following policy: Although the Japanese government adheres to the principle of non-interference in China's internal strife, if the Chinese side adopts non-friendly, anti-Japanese actions, it is prepared to take necessary measures. Therefore, if the new government threatens the lives and property of Japanese residents in the name of establishing tariff autonomy and abolishing unequal treaties, it will definitely take appropriate defensive measures. Furthermore, if there are political or military instigations by a third country behind the scenes, Japan cannot remain indifferent based on the spirit of the non-cession and non-exchange documents of Fujian. (Dentsu dispatch, 21st)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota, in view of the new program of the independent government of Fujian Province, which inevitably has communist and anti-Japanese colors, attaches great importance to the situation in Fujian Province. He immediately cabled the Consul General in Fuzhou, Moriya, and other Japanese officials stationed in Xiamen and other places, saying that Japan takes a non-interference policy on China's internal strife, but hopes that efforts will be made to protect the lives and property of Japanese residents. (Dentsu dispatch, 21st)

Shantou Bank Run Gradually Subsiding

(Shantou) There were rumors about the Provincial Bank branch's banknotes on the 19th. It happened to be Sunday, and the bank exceptionally opened for exchange, causing quite a run. There was still a run on the 20th, but it gradually subsided on the 21st. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Zhang Qun Summoned to Beijing: To Discuss Matters Regarding Fujian

(Hankou) Zhang Qun was summoned to Nanjing by telegram from Wang Jingwei to discuss important matters. Zhang is scheduled to take the Ning Shao steamer east on the evening of the 21st. Government affairs will be handled by the Chief Secretary Lu Zhu. (Special dispatch, 21st)

(Hankou) Because of the changes in Fujian Province, Wang summoned Zhang Qun by telegram on the 21st to discuss important plans. Zhang took the Wusong steamer to Beijing at 9:00 p.m. on the 21st. Military and political dignitaries boarded the ship to see him off. Zhang said that this trip was to discuss the current situation with Wang. He had not heard the truth about the Fujian incident. He should be able to get accurate information after arriving in Beijing. At a time when there is both internal strife and external threats, we must unite to survive. The changes made by Chen and others were unexpected. (Special dispatch, 21st)

(Hankou) Zhang Qun is going to Beijing to discuss the Fujian incident and will visit Chiang Kai-shek in Jiangxi on his way back to report on two matters: 1. The immigration of people from the border area was agreed upon with Liu Zhenhua, and he will ask for instructions on how to handle the refugee resettlement issue. 2. The Farmers' Bank of the Four Provinces will jointly issue ocean currency with the Hubei Provincial Bank and form a treasury with Shen Zhaonian as the treasurer, and will ask Chiang for instructions. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Chu Minyi Talks About the Fujian Incident

(Nanjing) Chu Minyi said that the Fujian incident had been brewing for a long time. When Chen Mingshu was in Hong Kong, there was talk of this. At that time, Mr. Hu Zhantang was also in Hong Kong and quite agreed. Later, Chen actually included the Third Party and democratic socialists to participate. People like Huang Qixiang and Zhang Bojun have already assumed important positions in Fujian. Hu, who hated evil as much as he hated an enemy, stopped his intention to enter Fujian. However, this Fujian incident is quite unwise. The Guangdong side and the central government have always been outwardly harmonious but inwardly divided. The sudden change in Fujian happened to give them an opportunity to unite. In addition to ordering military and political organs in various provinces and cities to take strict precautions, the central government does not need to send personnel to Fujian to investigate. Chiang Kai-shek has sent a telegram to transfer the central government's intentions. Chiang Kai-shek originally wanted to eliminate the trouble invisibly, so he specially sent a Sikes plane to Fujian to bring Cai Tingkai to Jiangxi for a trip so that he could explain in person. Unexpectedly, the Fujian side repeatedly prevaricated and detained the plane when the opportunity was ripe. As for confiscating the Central Bank and various agencies in Fujian, it is inevitable. As for how to deal with it, it depends on how the changes develop. However, it is expected that under the strict precautions on all sides, the situation will not be too great. Chu also said that the central government has now flown orders to the provincial and municipal governments and the garrisons in various places to pay close attention to and quickly deal with this disturbance. The Fujian Marine Corps and the navy stationed in Fujian were originally under the command of the Director of Pacification of Fujian. Now that Fujian has openly rebelled, the government has also ordered the navy and marine corps there to quickly deal with it and respond accordingly. The central government is now suppressing bandits and winning victories one after another. Chen and others have started a rebellion in Fujian Province and are sparing no effort to supply the Red bandits with food and salt, which is tantamount to helping the bandits do evil. The Red bandits, in their poverty, will naturally be happy to accept it, and perhaps they have a conspiracy to occupy Fujian Province and open up a sea outlet in the future. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Sun Ke Returns to Nanjing from Shanghai

(Nanjing) Sun Ke returned to Nanjing from Shanghai on the morning of the 21st. According to him, Yu and others went to Shanghai originally intending to eliminate the Fujian incident invisibly. Yesterday, we received a telegram from the central government urging us to return to Nanjing, so we took the night train to rush here. At the beginning of the brewing of the Fujian situation, the central government was based on the broad and tolerant intention to persuade them to dispel their delusions. Unexpectedly, Chen and others are now launching an attack in Fujian, and the central government has decided to deal with it severely. Someone asked what the Guangdong side would do about Fujian, Sun replied that Chen Jitang had taken precautions during the brewing of the Fujian situation and had transferred capable troops to guard the Guangdong-Fujian border. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Huang Shaoxiong: Preparing to Return to Nanjing to Report; Old Mongolian Areas in Suiyuan and Chahar Provinces: Will Establish Autonomous Region Governments; Qin Dechun Arrives in Suiyuan to Discuss Important Public Affairs

(Beiping) Huang Shaoxiong telegraphed from Beiping this morning, stating that the results of this trip to Bailingmiao to negotiate were satisfactory. Prince De and other princes have abandoned their original proposal to establish an autonomous government. The outline for resolving the Mongolian issue has also been decided. He will return to Beiping from Suiyuan within a few days to report to Nanjing. On the way back to Beiping, he plans to take a detour to Bingyuan to inspect the political situation in Shanxi Province. (Special dispatch, 21st)

(Guihua) According to Qin Dechun, who arrived in Suiyuan by special train from Zhangjiakou on the afternoon of the 21st, this visit was at Huang's invitation to discuss important matters. Song believes that as long as the central government makes a decision on the issue of Mongolian autonomy, he will absolutely obey. The Mongolian people's demand for autonomy is based on the meaning of equality of the five races and should be sympathized with and assisted to prevent the Mongolian people from going astray. If they separate from the central government, it is naturally unacceptable. It is planned to meet with Huang Zhuan tonight. Song can arrive in Beiping on the evening of the 21st. He has telegraphed to urge me to visit him, so I do not intend to stay in Suiyuan for long. I will go to Beiping on the 22nd to discuss the aftermath in Chahar Province. Tang's army is said to number 16,000. Since entering Chahar, the supplies have been enormous. Chahar has exhausted its financial resources and must quickly find a solution. Qin then went to the Xingyuan to meet with Zhao Pilian. (Special dispatch, 21st)

At 11:00 a.m. on the 20th, Prince Yun paid his respects to the Panchen Lama to bid farewell. He left the temple at 2:00 p.m. and returned to the prince's mansion. (Central News Agency dispatch, 21st)

At noon on the 21st, Prince De and Bao Yueqing and others paid their respects to the Panchen Lama to bid farewell. At 2:00 p.m., they left the temple and returned to the Wangfu of Yao Su Nite. (Central News Agency dispatch, 21st)

A joint celebration meeting is planned to be held in Suiyuan in the coming days. Chuan Zuoyi telegraphed to Prince De and others on the 19th, welcoming them to Suiyuan to communicate their feelings. Prince De said that he had been away from the banner for a long time and that the affairs of the league and banner needed to be sorted out. He returned to the prince's mansion at 2:00 p.m. on the 21st. (Central News Agency dispatch, 21st)

(Nanjing) A certain member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission said that the princes of various leagues and banners in Mongolia originally planned to gather the Mongolian people of Chahar and Suiyuan provinces to organize a Mongolian autonomous government, completely severing relations with the governments of Chahar and Suiyuan provinces. Later, Huang and Zhao personally went to Bailingmiao and sincerely persuaded and explained the righteousness. The princes understood the central government's painstaking efforts and no longer held their own opinions. They decided to abandon the autonomous government and follow the established principles, with slight changes. It is planned to establish an autonomous body for each of the Xilingol League in Chahar Province and the Ulanqab Yikezhao League in Suiyuan Province, which are in a parallel position with the provincial governments of Chahar and Suiyuan, and are still subject to the supervision and guidance of the central government to complete the outline of Mongolian local autonomy and improve the economic life of the Mongolian people. Although the outline was agreed upon by Huang, Zhao, and the princes, more detailed consultations will be made after arriving in Suiyuan, but the final decision will have to wait for Huang and Zhao to return to Nanjing and submit it to the Central Political Conference. The names of the agencies, the number of members, and the powers of the agencies will also be decided by the Central Political Conference. (Special dispatch, 21st)

(Nanjing) Huang Shaoxiong and Zhao Pilian telegraphed to Nanjing after arriving in Suiyuan, saying that the Mongolian affairs had been substantially resolved, and Prince De and others accepted the central government's intentions and voluntarily abandoned their preconceptions. From now on, the problem is only to properly plan and implement the measures in accordance with the established policy. All the details of the comforting process will be reported upon their return to Nanjing. (Special dispatch, 21st)

(Beiping) Zhao Nasatu and five other representatives who returned to Beiping from Bailingmiao gave a detailed account of the Bailingmiao meeting. Autonomous region governments will be established in the old Mongolian areas of Suiyuan and Chahar provinces. The names will be the First Autonomous Region Government of Mongolia and the Second Autonomous Region Government of Mongolia. There is no conflict with the two provinces of Huan and Cha. The rest can be inferred by analogy. The First District of Mongolia is the Ulanqab League, the Yikezhao League, and the Matte Independent Banner. The Second District is the Xilingol League, the Chahar League, and the Feng Autonomous Region Governments. They are directly under the Executive Yuan of the Central Government. In the event of matters involving provinces and counties, they will be handled jointly with the provincial government. The Mongolian autonomous region governments will manage all political affairs of each alliance and banner within their respective regions. Each autonomous region will have a chairman, two vice-chairmen, and two to four full-time members. The head of each banner will be an ex officio member. According to the actual situation, departments and offices will be established to take charge of the autonomous region government. A joint meeting will be established, and each autonomous region and each banner may send one representative to organize it to discuss and decide on matters of common concern to each autonomous region. The expenses of the autonomous region government will be directly allocated by the central government. The details will have to wait for the Executive Yuan to submit detailed discussions, which will be reviewed by the Legislative Yuan and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review: 1. The candidates for chairman, vice-chairmen, and full-time members of the First and Second Autonomous Regions. 2. Detailed rules for the internal organization of the autonomous region. 3. The amount of funds for the autonomous region government. 4. The management method of Mongolian and Han people in the counties established in Sui and Cha. The counties established in Mongolian areas are mostly inhabited by both Mongolian and Han people. The original livelihood land tax issues of the Mongolian people, as well as the areas that have not yet been enclosed into counties, will be discussed and decided. Most of the Mongolian lands are used for grazing and production by the Mongolian people. Areas that have not yet been enclosed into counties will be stopped and used exclusively as pastures. The issue of tax revenue in the Mongolian areas of the counties established in Sui and Cha will be jointly managed by the Sui and Cha provincial governments and the first and second autonomous region governments, adopting an equal distribution policy. Predetermined policies for the first and second autonomous region governments: 1. Agriculture: implement land reclamation and afforestation. 2. Grazing: improve grazing industry using scientific methods. 3. Industry: exploit minerals and manufacture leather and fur products. 4. Transportation: each league and banner will implement the construction of motor vehicle companies to connect traffic and railways. Railways will not be established temporarily due to factual and economic reasons. 5. Post: consult with the Ministry of Communications to implement postal services in various places. 6. Education: adopt two types: A. Military education; B. Vocational education. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Anglo-Franco-American-Italian Understanding: Overall Resolution of the European Situation, Disarmament Conference Recesses for Negotiations with Germany, League of Nations Covenant Expected to Undergo Major Revision

(Geneva) After continuing discussions on disarmament issues with representatives of the major powers in Geneva today, the Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, has convened the main committee to meet on Wednesday. The major powers have designated a drafting committee to prepare a proposal for the general committee to adjourn until after the League of Nations Executive Council meeting on January 10th, and then reconvene. Simultaneously, the technical committee will continue for another seven or eight days after the adjournment. During this period, governments, including Germany, will exchange diplomatic documents to clarify the situation. It is reported that the negotiations will extend beyond the structure of the Disarmament Conference. The most important powers will meet in January next year. It is rumored that significant progress has been made, and even French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour is satisfied with the progress of the discussions.

British Foreign Secretary Simon is leaving for London tonight, but will return to Geneva if necessary. Judging by appearances, the main committee will adjourn on Wednesday, and Simon may not need to return. British Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs, Eden, will remain in Geneva as the British representative. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol is leaving for Rome tonight, ostensibly to attend Schanzer's funeral, but it is widely believed that Avenol will discuss Italy's attitude towards the League of Nations.

The issue of Henderson's resignation was not mentioned during today's disarmament discussions. It appears that Henderson's strong words regarding the conference have had an effect, and he views the current adjournment as something that cannot be delayed.

It is widely believed that British Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Geneva has cleared the air. Paul-Boncour claims that the attitudes of Britain and France are now closer than before. According to general opinion, the exchange of diplomatic documents offers the best opportunity for genuine progress. The so-called negotiation scope extending beyond the Disarmament Conference implies that the reorganization of the League of Nations and the future of the Saar region will also be discussed. If so, the upcoming conference will be different from the Disarmament Conference. No wonder there are rumors that the conference will be held in Italy. (Reuters, 20th)

(Geneva) This afternoon, after consultations between the four major powers, they have agreed in principle to suspend the work of the Disarmament Conference pending private negotiations with Germany. However, the final decision will await a renewed meeting of the representatives of Britain, the United States, France, and Italy today, before being submitted to the Main Committee meeting tomorrow for approval. It is reported that there is no longer a question about the four major powers and Germany immediately starting negotiations in Italy. The duration of the Disarmament Conference's adjournment is expected to be decided today. It is anticipated that the conference will be suspended until the end of January. At that time, the British, French, and Italian governments will, through their diplomatic representatives, separately discuss and agree on the date and location for private negotiations with Germany. It is reported that Italian representative De Suella has not yet notified other countries' representatives of the Italian Prime Minister's invitation to negotiate in Rome, but observers believe that as soon as the Disarmament Conference decides to suspend proceedings, De Suella will issue this invitation. Tonight, a spokesman for the American delegation announced that during yesterday's four-country consultation, American representative Wilson formally proposed expanding the scope of private talks to include other countries. Chairman Henderson expressed his support, but was opposed by representatives from Italy, Britain, and France. It is understood that the countries the United States wants to invite to join are clearly Japan and Soviet Russia. (National Telegram, 20th)

Avenol Visits Mussolini for Negotiations: Plan to Reorganize League of Nations, Separation of Covenant from Treaty of Versailles, Allowing the US, Russia, Germany, and Japan to Join

(Geneva) The situation of Italy's withdrawal from the League of Nations has become so serious that it necessitates a special visit by League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. Furthermore, it is reported that a major plan to reorganize the structure of the League of Nations is currently under consideration. Avenol departs for Rome tonight, ostensibly to attend the funeral of former Italian Foreign Minister and Chairman of the League of Nations Executive Council in 1929, Schanzer. However, according to reliable sources, his true purpose is to persuade Mussolini not to withdraw from the League of Nations. Key figures in diplomatic circles here have verified that Avenol's sudden decision to travel to Rome came after receiving confidential information about Italy's attitude. A diplomat familiar with the inner workings of the League of Nations also stated that politicians in this region and in Europe and America all recognize the threat of Italy's withdrawal from the League of Nations as a most serious problem. Although the claim that a plan to reorganize the League of Nations is under consideration has been denied by a highly involved individual, reliable sources are deeply aware that a major change in the structure and policies of the League of Nations is currently being planned. The denial by the individual is probably because they fear that premature disclosure would hinder progress. It is reported that the goal of this reorganization is to make the power of the League of Nations more universal and to make it easier to handle world problems. It was recently learned from an extremely reliable source that before going to Rome, Avenol consulted Belgian legal expert Paul Hymans, who currently serves as the Belgian representative to the Disarmament Conference and a professor at the Geneva Institute of International Studies, on the method of revising the covenant and reorganizing the League. It is reported that Hymans has drafted a new reorganization plan, but Hymans himself denied it tonight, only admitting that Avenol had sought his opinion on the revision issue. However, those close to Hymans insist that he has drafted a plan to separate the League of Nations Covenant from the Treaty of Versailles, and to greatly revise the Covenant, expanding the purpose of the League of Nations while reducing the guarantee of treaty obligations, allowing the US, Russia, Germany, and Japan to join. In addition, it is proposed to expand the number of members of the Executive Council, establish an executive committee, and reduce the number of secret meetings of the League of Nations Assembly. As for the military arbitration in Article 16 of the current Covenant, it may be deleted in Hymans's new proposal. Italian sources here believe that Avenol may present this reorganization plan to Mussolini in an attempt to persuade Italy to remain in the League of Nations. (National Telegram, 20th)

Mussolini's Bold Words: Views League of Nations as a Patient; Italy Has No Intention of Hastily Leaving the Sickbed

Rome: Prime Minister Mussolini has declared to the French ambassador that his policies do not intend to break away from the League of Nations. The Grand Council of Fascism will discuss the relationship between Italy and the League of Nations on December 5th, but this is merely a routine procedure. This is the first meeting of the Grand Council of Fascism since Germany withdrew from the League of Nations. A year ago, when the council discussed the League of Nations issue, Prime Minister Mussolini said that the League of Nations is now a patient and Italy should not stay away from the sickbed. The general public here believes that if Italy were to withdraw from the League of Nations, the friendly relations between Britain and Italy would inevitably become strained. (Reuters, 20th)

Britain and Italy Initiate Discussion of a New International Conference to Discuss Important World Political Issues

(Geneva) According to widely circulated but completely unconfirmed reports here today, British Prime Minister MacDonald or Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will soon convene a new international conference to discuss important global political issues. Participants will be limited to a selection of major and minor powers, including the United States, Soviet Russia, and Japan. The issues to be discussed will primarily be the reorganization of the League of Nations, revision of the Covenant, and the issue of League of Nations mandated territories. (National Telegram, 21st)

Rome: According to informed sources here today, the Fascist leader will take the opportunity of the Fascist Grand Council meeting in early December to formally express Italy's position on the League of Nations. Regarding rumors that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will redefine his foreign policy, the authorities have firmly stated that the general direction will not change, but will advocate first convening a conference of major powers, and then convening a disarmament conference to seriously engage in work. (National Telegram, 20th)

(Paris) According to a telegram from a Paris Evening News correspondent in Geneva, the "Small Disarmament Conference" will likely be held in San Remo, Italy, as soon as possible. French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour intends to participate. The participants will not only be the signatory countries of the Four-Power Pact, but also countries with direct relations to Franco-German amity, such as Soviet Russia, Poland, Belgium, and the Little Entente. (National Telegram, 20th)

(Geneva) It is certain that Germany and the four major powers will immediately begin negotiations in Italy, but it is expected that Britain, France, and Italy will still arrange a transitional meeting through their ambassadors to Germany, so that the Disarmament Conference can proceed quickly when it reconvenes. (National Telegram, 21st)

(Geneva) There are rumors here that the Disarmament Conference may be held outside of Geneva, with Germany participating. We initially reported on this matter yesterday, but whether this is practical or a trial balloon remains to be seen. However, practically speaking, our representative received confirmation from the most reliable American sources this morning that British Foreign Secretary Simon, before returning to London, had sounded out the American representative on the attitude the American government would take if Britain or Italy proposed holding the Disarmament Conference outside of Geneva. We have further learned that Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson made similar inquiries to Soviet representative Dovgalevsky. Diplomatic circles here are surprised to learn that Henderson has made this contact, as it seems inappropriate for Henderson personally to abandon Geneva and hold a European conference in an Italian city. The explanation for Henderson's actions is that he has received assurances from the British and Italian governments, or perhaps even from the German government, that he will still have a role to play, for example, chairing the disarmament committee at this European conference. In addition, Henderson has been assured that regardless of the outcome of this conference, the Geneva Disarmament Conference will still be discussed, or at least recognized. What is practical is only so much. Beyond that, once the date and agenda of the European conference are mentioned, there is no shortage of ambiguity and conjecture. Thinking carefully, even if such a conference is successful, it may not be held within this year or early next year. Because the major powers decided yesterday to seek a solution to the Disarmament Conference through diplomatic channels, this will not be accomplished in a day or a month. Considering the negotiations for the Four-Power Pact took several weeks, it is known that the future Disarmament Convention will also take a long time to come to fruition. As for the agenda of the European conference, it is reported that the organizers intend for this conference to have a broader agenda than the Disarmament Conference, and its nature is almost a peace conference, in other words, a conference to revise existing treaties. As such, it is difficult to say whether such a conference can be held before Britain or Italy expresses a clear view. However, there is strong opposition to this plan in various countries, especially Poland and the Little Entente countries, who do not want to hear about a European conference involving the revision of existing treaties. Therefore, this plan may not make progress in the coming days, but Britain will maintain this view and continue to explore, and because this proposition has been widely leaked, Britain's ability to act is becoming increasingly cautious. (Havas, 21st)

France Strengthens Border Defenses

(Paris) The French Army Committee, convened to draft a plan for the reorganization of the army, has submitted a request to Prime Minister Sarraut to quickly complete the great defense project along the Franco-German border. (National Telegram, 21st)

Speech at the Opening of Parliament: British Monarch Supports League of Nations; Continues Cooperation with Other Countries to Maintain Peace

(London) Parliament opened today, and the British monarch delivered a speech, stating that the British government's greatest interest is to promote world peace and maintain it with all its strength. The British government will continue to cooperate with other governments to seek a satisfactory solution to the complex issue of disarmament, so as to establish a method acceptable to all parties and achieve the satisfactory conclusion of the Disarmament Conference's long-term work. The British government is determined to maintain the work of international cooperation through the League of Nations mechanism and other methods that can promote good relations between countries and peoples. He then said that he hoped that the Joint Committee on the Indian Constitution could complete its hard work in a timely manner so that practical proposals could be submitted to Parliament in the form of legislation during this parliamentary session. The British monarch then spoke of British industry and commerce, saying that a noteworthy development in the past year was the gradual restoration of confidence in the future of British industry and commerce, which should be maintained and promoted. Cabinet members are carefully paying attention to the sound principle of controlling spending and adopting plans that can encourage enterprise, striving to enable the country to return to a state where the burden on the people can be lightened. Cabinet members will also continue to work to create an environment conducive to export trade, through negotiating trade agreements, hoping to obtain opportunities to develop the cotton, coal, and other export industries. Regarding the unemployment problem, the government will propose a fundamentally sound unemployment insurance plan and establish a system to assist unemployed people not covered by this insurance. (Reuters, 21st)

American Envoy to Arrive in Shantou Soon

(Shantou) The American Consul in Shantou has invited political, military, and business leaders to participate in a grand event for the visit of the American Minister to China, Johnson, and the commander of the Asian Fleet to Shantou. Johnson will come to Shantou. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Freedom in a Democratic Nation: Labor Party Member Formerly Imprisoned, Now Vigorously Speaks in Parliament

(London) Today, after the British monarch finished delivering his speech in Parliament, left-wing Labor Party member McGovern shouted loudly, "What about the means test for unemployment benefits? It is a disgrace that people are starving to death!" McGovern made this statement, gesticulating to express his disapproval of the solemn and magnificent scene in Parliament. However, the British monarch and queen paid no attention and left the venue in order. McGovern is a former sheet metal worker, then a foreman, and in 1930 became an insurance agent. He was elected to Parliament that year. He has been ordered to leave the chamber repeatedly for causing trouble for the Speaker. In 1931, he was imprisoned for speaking recklessly outside and participating in unemployment riots. (Reuters, 21st)

(London) Today, when the British monarch delivered the opening speech to Parliament in the House of Lords, Member of Parliament McGovern suddenly interrupted, shouting, "How will unemployment be solved? You lazy parasites, living on the wealth created by others, should be ashamed. Think of the people outside who are starving to death!" Afterwards, McGovern told reporters, "I have no regrets. I was extremely indignant at the time." (National Telegram, 21st)

Japan Becomes a World of Assassination: Wakatsuki Narrowly Escapes Two Assassination Attempts Yesterday Morning; Attacked First at Ueno Station and Later in Yamato Village; Assailants Were a Martial Artist and a Retired Soldier, Both Arrested; Assassination Motivated by Opposition to London Naval Treaty

(Tokyo) An assassination attempt on Wakatsuki, the chief Japanese delegate to the London Naval Conference, failed this morning. Wakatsuki had just returned to Tokyo from somewhere this morning. As he was getting off the train, a young man, wielding a dagger, broke through the crowd and attempted to assassinate him, but was apprehended by the police before he could reach Wakatsuki.

Wakatsuki has served as Prime Minister twice, Minister of Finance twice, Minister of Home Affairs once, and Vice Minister of Finance twice, making him a prominent figure in Japanese politics. He has narrowly escaped danger several times because ardent Japanese patriots believe that his signing of the naval ratio agreement damaged Japan's national defense and branded him as a traitor. The assailant this morning was Noguchi, a famous Japanese martial artist. At the same time, another young man also attempted an assassination, but had already fled when the police arrived. It is reported that today's incident is related to the recent movement against the London Naval Treaty.

The assailant who escaped with Noguchi after the unsuccessful assassination attempt on Wakatsuki this morning later loitered outside Wakatsuki's residence, attempting a second assassination, and was arrested by the police in front of the house. His name is Matsui. Both assailants are members of a reactionary organization. However, according to Noguchi, he was implicated in the May 15th Incident and other cases, and naval cadets have recently undergone military trials, so he was angered by the naval treaty and attempted to assassinate Wakatsuki, and was not in collusion with Matsui. However, Noguchi has confessed that he and Matsui recently purchased daggers specifically to assassinate Wakatsuki. (Reuters, 21st)

Two Unsuccessful Assassination Attempts

(Tokyo) Wakatsuki Reijiro, the president of the Minseito party, attended a party conference in the Hokushin area. He was returning to Tokyo on the 21st and arrived at Ueno Station at 7:00 AM. As he exited the gate and was about to get into his car, a ruffian suddenly jumped out of the crowd, wielding a short sword, intending to stab Wakatsuki. However, he was arrested by escorting police officers before he could approach Wakatsuki. After Wakatsuki returned home, he took a train from Ueno Station to his Izu villa at 8:40 AM. (Jiji Press, 21st)

(Tokyo) The assailant who attempted to assassinate Wakatsuki, Matsui Haruo, fled upon seeing Noguchi's arrest, but went all the way to Wakatsuki's residence in Hongo Yamato Village, attempting to carry out the attack again. He was discovered in front of the house and arrested. Matsui retired from the military this October and often talked about patriotic issues. (Jiji Press, 21st)

Wakatsuki Remains Calm

Atami: Wakatsuki, who narrowly escaped disaster at Ueno Station, took a train from Tokyo Station to his villa in Ito at 9:05 AM. He got off the train at Atami Station, and said the following, "Wherever I go, if I am destined to suffer, there is no way to avoid it. Therefore, I am always fully prepared. So, whether to help or not is irrelevant, let fate decide." Wakatsuki remained quite calm after this near-death experience. (Jiji Press, 21st)

(Tokyo) Wakatsuki Reijiro, who was attacked twice this morning at his residence and Ueno Station, said at his residence that life and death are in the hands of Heaven, and that he has dedicated his life to the country. He spoke calmly, as usual. Wakatsuki still went to Ito at 9:05 AM for rest, as planned, and intends to stay there for a week. (Denstu, 21st)

Assailant's Motive

(Tokyo) After the Metropolitan Police Department arrested the assailant who attacked Wakatsuki, they conducted a thorough interrogation. The assailant's name is Noguchi Susumu, 27 years old, a heavyweight boxer belonging to the Japan Boxing Club founded by Kano Kenjiro in Hyogo Prefecture. He was injured in the ribs during a recent match against a British Asian Fleet athlete, and came to Tokyo from Hyogo Prefecture. He is quite violent and has committed assault crimes. The authorities are currently investigating the purpose and motive of his attack, and the relationship behind it. A letter of advice was found in his possession. There is another assailant who escaped into the crowd when he saw that the purpose was not achieved. The authorities are vigorously searching for his whereabouts. Also, it is reported that the assailants who attempted to assassinate Wakatsuki were Noguchi Susumu and Matsui Haruo, both members of the Patriotic Youth League, which was founded by Lin Itiro, the lawyer for the naval defendants in the May 15th Incident. (Jiji Press)

(Tokyo) According to police investigation, Noguchi Susumu came to Tokyo from Kobe on October 8th. On the 6th of this month, regarding the Sagoya case of assassination of Prime Minister Hamaguchi, he listened to the case in court, and discussed the case with his friend Matsui Haruo, saying that Sagoya's death sentence was a result of the failure of the London Treaty, and that Baron Wakatsuki should commit seppuku to atone for his crime. He decided to advise Wakatsuki and urge him to commit suicide. He discussed this with Matsui several times, and arranged to hand over the letter of advice when Wakatsuki departed from Ueno Station on the 19th of this month, and to carry out extortion. He purchased two short swords. On the 21st, at 6:45 AM, he waited for Wakatsuki at Ueno Station. Noguchi produced the letter of advice and a short sword and was threatening him when he was arrested by the police. At that time, Matsui chased after the car that Wakatsuki was riding in and was arrested by the police. It is reported that the police intend to charge Noguchi with extortion. The main contents of the letter of advice held by Noguchi are as follows: "Sagoya was sentenced to death, which was the result of the failure of the London Treaty, and Baron Wakatsuki should commit seppuku to atone for his crime." (Jiji Press, 21st)

(Tokyo) Noguchi Susumu, at the Metropolitan Police Department, has consistently denied any relationship with right-wing groups and any behind-the-scenes mastermind, and confessed that he had this act because he was angered by the London Treaty. However, the authorities believe that Kano Kenjiro, the president of the Japan Boxing Association, was the mastermind behind him and are conducting an investigation. (Jiji Press, 21st)

(Tokyo) The true intention of Noguchi Susumu in attacking Baron Wakatsuki was not to assassinate Wakatsuki, but to advise him to commit seppuku, but the incident seems to have been organized by a group, so the Metropolitan Police Department is making every effort to search for the mastermind behind the scenes, and as a result, a second Blood Pledge Corps may be discovered. (Denstu, 21st)

(Tokyo) Iwata Ainosuke, the head of the Aikoku-sha, spoke as follows regarding the assassination attempt on Wakatsuki, the president of the Minseito party: Noguchi and Matsui were previously members of our company. Noguchi became a boxer four or five years ago, and Matsui joined the Taiwan Independence Garrison, and their relationship with the Aikoku-sha has been severed. At the boxing tournament at the end of October, Noguchi suddenly visited, and at that time he thought that his thinking had not changed. (Denstu, 21st)

Japan's Siberian Intervention: Litvinov Implies in Speech That Demand for Damages Will Not Be Abandoned

(Tokyo) The terms of the current resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia are more favorable and extensive than those agreed with other countries. The most notable is that Soviet Russia abandoned its claim for damages suffered due to the United States' intervention in Siberia in 1918. According to Ambassador Debuchi's report on the 20th, the reason for this is that Soviet Russia indicated that Japan's intervention in Siberia was an illegal act. According to Ambassador Debuchi's report, Litvinov stated at the Washington News Association on the day of the establishment of the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia, that the reason why the Soviet Union abandoned the right to claim damages for the United States' intervention in Siberia was that when he visited the State Department, he admitted that the United States' intervention was an act for which the Soviet Union should be grateful. According to the explanation of the United States' intervention, the purpose of the United States' intervention was not to fight the extremists, but to protect Russian territory and monitor the Japanese army. Japan's intervention was a military intervention to prevent the Soviet Russian labor revolution. In other words, Japan's Siberian intervention was due to a counter-revolutionary military intervention. Litvinov implied in his words that the Soviet Union would not abandon the claim for damages for Japan's intervention. If negotiations on debt and credit issues are established between the United States and Russia, then Japan, based on the Japanese-Russian Basic Treaty of Yoshizawa-Karakhan, would naturally enjoy the same benefits. However, Litvinov's words and actions deliberately prevented Japan from enjoying this benefit. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs recognizes that Litvinov's statement denies the explicit text of the Japanese-Russian Basic Agreement and attaches great importance to the future. (Jiji Press, 21st)

Rome: It is reported that Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov, after agreeing with US President Roosevelt on the Russian-American resumption of diplomatic relations treaty, is currently still in the United States and is scheduled to travel to Rome on the 25th of this month aboard an Italian postal ship, and then return to Russia from Rome. (Havas, 21st)

U.S.-Russia Aviation Agreement: U.S. Engineers to Russia to Establish Aircraft Manufacturing Plant

(Harbin) It is heard that United Airlines of the United States and the Soviet Russian government have signed a contract to establish an aircraft manufacturing plant in Soviet Russia. A large number of American technicians have already been dispatched. Furthermore, American military supply manufacturers, recruited by Soviet Russia, have sent many outstanding experts to Soviet Russia. (Telegraph from the 21st) According to the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun of the 14th, the American Notification News announced on the 12th that the U.S. and Russia had reached an agreement to establish and assist an aircraft plant. The report stated that representatives of the Soviet Russian Federation and the American Curtis-Wright Aeronautical Corporation had discussed establishing an aircraft plant in Russia. The plant will be under American supervision and is expected to be completed soon. This plan has been approved by the U.S. Army and Navy to assist in Soviet Russia's five-year plan to expand military and commercial aviation. Specifically regarding the eastern border, Moscow's response hinted at coercing Japan. It is heard that the American company can earn millions of dollars annually from this plan. In addition to Curtis-Wright's president, Mr. Mulheron, taking full responsibility for guidance, the Budd Wheel Company will also dispatch several supervisors to Russia.

U.S. Streamlines Tax Revenue: Annual Increase of 300 to 400 Million Dollars

(Washington) According to sources today, the national tax law is currently being revised. As a result, the national income tax revenue will increase by 300 to 400 million dollars annually without increasing income tax rates. The plan proposed by the House Ways and Means Committee advocates for the repeal of all changes to income tax laws since 1920. Various exceptions currently enjoyed by individuals and companies may be entirely abolished. The Ways and Means Committee, chaired by Democrat Hill, will submit its detailed report, the result of a week's research, to the tax experts of the bicameral Joint Committee on Internal Revenue Taxation for review. Whether companies can continue to file consolidated reports is also a question the Ways and Means Committee wants to submit to the bicameral committee for review. The bicameral Joint Committee on Internal Revenue Taxation is scheduled to meet on December 4 to review the current practice of deducting 50% for depreciation and liquidation purposes, as well as the required amount for debt repayment. These points will also be discussed in the report. Hill predicts that if the Ways and Means Committee's proposal is passed by Congress, the nation can collect an additional 300 to 400 million dollars in income tax annually without raising taxes, as individuals and companies will have to pay income tax on all actual income. As for the losses reported in the current year, they can be deducted from income. (Reuter's telegram from the 20th)

(Washington) According to a report today, since the U.S. government began buying gold domestically in the most recent week of October, it has collected a total of 265,000 ounces of cash, paying a price of $7.55 million. As for gold purchased in Europe, the amount is minimal, limited to activities in London and Paris. (Reuter's telegram from the 20th)

Where Did the Earthquake Strike? London Meteorological Observatory Has Records, Location Unconfirmed

(London) Yesterday at 11:28 PM, the Meteorological Observatory's seismograph recorded a violent earthquake. Its epicenter was either in the Black Sea, the Caspian Sea, or at the 140th meridian. Seismologist Moren confirmed that when London recorded the earthquake for sixty minutes, the needle on the seismograph swayed a maximum distance of ten inches, indicating the severity of the tremor. A seismologist at the West Bromwich Meteorological Observatory expressed the opinion that the epicenter was very close to England, and that the earthquake was felt worldwide last night. According to a Reuter's reporter in London, the Black Sea earthquake theory has not been verified. A Reuter's reporter in Sydney also telegraphed, stating that they recorded an earthquake at the same time as London last night, estimating its epicenter to be on a straight line between New Guinea and Japan. A Reuter's reporter in Victoria, British Columbia, telegraphed, reporting that the local meteorological observatory recorded an earthquake, its severity being unprecedented. According to their report, the epicenter was 2,300 miles away, approximately in Mexico or Siberia. (Reuter's telegram from the 21st)

Measures for the Exhibition of Mongol and Tibetan Political and Religious Leaders in Nanjing; Regulations by the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission

Xu Prefecture Requests Closure of the Hanzhuang Sluice Gate

(Xuzhou) The Xuzhou Administrative Inspector's Office received a report from the Tongshan and Pi counties and the Weishan Lake Fishermen's Self-Defense Corps, stating that the county magistrate of Teng County had recently personally led a large number of police and soldiers to remove nine sections of the ear boards from the Hanzhuang Sluice Gate, through which the Weishan Canal passes, causing the lake water to flow wildly towards the canal. The counties of Pi and Sui in the lower reaches will suffer damage. The motive for opening the gate was a secret agreement between Teng and Pei counties to release the lake water and prepare to dry up the surrounding lake fields. Commissioner She Nianci reported that Weishan Lake is located between Jiangsu and Shandong provinces and is situated in the lower reaches. The terrain is the lowest, and all the waters of Shandong flow to this lake. This time, Teng County removed the gate panels, and the residents along the lake and on both sides of the Central Canal have lost all protection. The release of Shandong water into the lake has increased the volume of water, which will inevitably overflow into the canal. If there is continuous rain or the flood season in the coming summer and autumn, the counties of Tongshan, Pi, Sui, and Suqian will suffer greatly. He has telegraphed a report to the provincial government, requesting that it consult the Shandong provincial government and order Teng County to close the gate quickly. Letter from the Embassy in Cuba

To the Editor: Your newspaper published a special dispatch from Nanjing on September 12, dated September 11, stating, "Cuba is excluding overseas Chinese, blockading property, and deporting them. Envoy Ling has lodged a protest. The Cuban government has refused to meet with him. Ling has telegraphed to request the remittance of 20,000 yuan as travel expenses for overseas Chinese returning home, but the government has not agreed." After investigation, Cuba is currently in turmoil, and overseas Chinese have suffered some losses, but there is no exclusion, blockade, or deportation. Since the establishment of the new Cuban government, our government has not recognized it, so Envoy Ling has not formally visited any Cuban government agency. As for the request for a remittance of 20,000 yuan, it did not happen. We hereby request your newspaper to make a correction. We would be very grateful. To the Shanghai Shenbao Newspaper, From the Embassy in Cuba, October 24.

Jiang Re-Orders Sichuan Troops to Vigorously Coordinate and Suppress Bandits; Liu Xiang Orders General Offensive; Xu's Bandits Retreat Entirely North; Xu Yuanquan Returns to Shashi, Proceeding to the Front to Oversee Suppression of He's Bandits

Hankou Correspondence: Xu Xiang's remnant bandits, fleeing eastward from northern Sichuan, attacked and raided Tian Songyao, Yang Sen, Liu Cunhou, and other units successively, like a strong wind sweeping leaves, with unstoppable ferocity. Liu Xiang's defense area was also threatened, and Kaiwan was alarmed for a time, shaking the entire Sichuan. After the Fifth Route Army under Wang Lingji and the Sixth Route Army under Fan Shaozeng received orders to attack, they engaged in bloody battles with the bandit army led by He Wei and others between Kaijiang and Suiding, in the battles of Sanhuikou, Huilongchang, Yongxingchang, and other engagements. Both sides used their main forces to confront each other. The bandits were unsuccessful, and their eastward plan suffered a setback. They retreated with their main force to Luojiangkou between Suixuan, and Fan pursued them, leading to another fierce battle. Liu Xiang, seeing military success, issued a general offensive order on the sixteenth, charging Wang and Fan's armies to advance from Suixuan, Yang Sen to advance from Yingshan, and also ordering Deng Xihou to quickly concentrate at Zhaoguang and join Tian Songyao in an eastward advance to achieve an enveloping effect. It had long been rumored that Suiding and Yingshan had been recovered, but based on the facts, it seems they are still in the hands of the bandits. What has been recovered is only their subordinate territories. Chairman Chiang, based on a telegram presented by the Sichuan Province People's Anti-Bandit Support Association, stating that Wang and Fan's units had been in fierce battles with the bandits for many days and other units had not yet advanced, telegraphed Liu Xiang again, ordering him to immediately relay orders to all armies, to coordinate effectively and suppress the bandits simultaneously, and to avoid waiting and watching, falling into the bandits' plan of defeating them one by one. It is heard that the bandit troops between Suixuan began to retreat entirely north on the eighteenth. Those guarding Pujiaochang have retreated towards Zhongxing and Yangliu, and the baggage and supplies at Yanmen are also moving towards Yixing. The eastern front of the war is gradually becoming calm, and the National Army seems to be able to take the entire territory of Suixuan without a fight. However, the war on the northern front suddenly became tense. On the line of Zhaoguang, Canglang, bandits and Tian's army have been in contact for days, and war clouds are gathering on the banks of the Jialing River. It seems that the bandits, failing to achieve their goals on the eastern front, are directing their entire force northward, intending to take advantage of Deng's army not having arrived to break through Tian's army while it is weak. Tian's units comprise six divisions and five routes, about more than thirty regiments, mostly gathered in Canglang. Although they have suffered repeated setbacks, their morale is very firm, and they know the bandits' tricks very well, so they can still hold on. A few days ago, Tian Songyao stated that if the bandits invade, he will definitely not allow them to cross the defense line, but before Deng's units are concentrated, it will not be easy to launch an isolated offensive. The bandits He Long and Xia Xi, being夹擊 by the Sichuan and Hubei armies, have an even stronger desire to enter Sichuan. They are currently entrenched in Qianli, straddling Sichuan and Hubei, with the intention of invading Yunyang and Fengjie. Liu Xiang has ordered the Sichuan East armies and newly formed teams to strictly block them, preventing them from crossing the Yangtze River and linking up with Xu's bandits. Xu Yuanquan is responsible for overseeing the suppression of these bandits and flew back to Shashi from Hankou on the twentieth, immediately departing for Enshi to督师 (oversee the troops). (Twentieth)

Xuzhou: Tragedy Amidst Paper Money Crisis; Party and Government Establish Paper Money Clearing Office; People Rush to Exchange, Trampling and Injuring Pregnant Woman

Xuzhou Correspondence: Since the outbreak of the private paper money crisis in Xuzhou, the party and government authorities have repeatedly sought ways to maintain and clear it. However, the seven combined only established one public exchange office in the Chamber of Commerce. Those exchanging cash were packed like sardines, leading to repeated incidents. Although the party and government authorities recently established a Paper Money Clearing Association, the tragedy of people rushing to exchange cash occurred. Although paper money circulation in the market has eased slightly, public opinion is greatly agitated by the tragedy. Details are recorded below:

Clearing Paper Money

The people of Xuzhou have suffered from the poison of paper money for a long time. A thorough ban is the unanimous demand. In the past few years, merchants issuing paper money, whenever facing public criticism, would seek assistance from the administrative authorities, offering a considerable sum of money to maintain the issuance of paper money. Administrative personnel also used this public opinion as a means of reaping benefits. Therefore, although there have been several organizations of financial reorganization committees, the issuance of private paper money continued as before. Now, at the time of the paper money collapse, all sectors advocate a thorough clearing. The county government has invited the county reorganization committee, the first district office, the Chamber of Commerce, and the silver and money industry association to establish a Paper Money Clearing Committee, which began working at the county government office on the nineteenth. Those responsible are County Magistrate She Nianci, Rui Zhenxiang of the county reorganization committee, Chen Xizhe of the first district office, Lan Bohua of the Chamber of Commerce, and Zhang Junchuan of the silver and money industry. The implementation methods are as follows: (1) The seven private money houses, except for Gongyu, which is a joint stock company and is separately cleared by the shareholders, the remaining Chunquan, Bu Xinjie, Yi Zhenxiang, Shi Xingchang, Ju Hechang, and Tian Bao Yu, their existing paper money will be investigated, sealed, and destroyed on a fixed date. (2) The paper money continuously exchanged and collected by each house will be sealed and destroyed daily. (3) The printing plates stored in each money house will be collected, sealed, and stored. (4) External affairs will be handled by the county government, and county government officials will be assigned to keep the case files. Each committee member is already proceeding with the prescribed matters separately. As for the shareholders of Gongyu 銀號, they were also convened by the county government yesterday to discuss. More than forty people attended, and the President of the Chamber of Commerce, Lan Bohua, and Xie You'an from the silver and money industry also attended. Chairman She Nianci ordered each shareholder to bear unlimited liability and quickly raise funds to clear the exchanges, awarding the organization of the Gongyu Clearing Office. Gao Yuru, Zhang Xiangchen, Du Yushan, Li Aitang, Cai Wenzhi, Zhou Jiyu, Li Xingzhou, Chen Zhonghao, Zhuang Shaojiu, and Sun Yipeng were appointed as eleven committee members responsible for clearing. The regulations are: (1) Gongyu's existing receipts and loans will be requested by the county government to be collected, and the floating loans on the account will be collected by the Clearing Office. (2) Shareholders will borrow funds from banks with collateral to issue and exchange paper money, and the Clearing Office will be responsible for negotiation. (3) The existing paper money, approximately 800,000 strings, will be verified by the Clearing Office and publicly destroyed. (4) Uncollected paper money will be uniformly cleared by the Clearing Office, sealed daily, and awaiting destruction. Each committee member has already started handling the matter. Coupled with the lack of cash in the market, the paper money of other money houses, except for Gongyu, has slightly eased in the market these days. However, it is by no means purely trust, but because private paper money has been holding the market for a long time, there is almost no other way to operate. The deeply rooted roots and the severity of the poison can be imagined.

Tragedy of Rushing to Exchange

The Public Exchange Office is located in the Chamber of Commerce. The seven combined only raised several hundred yuan of cash each day, while the paper money outside totaled more than two million. How could this be enough? The exchange time is from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM and from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, only four hours temporarily. With seven houses gathered in one place, the people holding paper money came in droves, which was even more insufficient to distribute. In recent days, tragedies have been staged repeatedly. Even with military and police maintaining order and armed suppression on the scene, it is easy to cause incidents. Every day, several members of the public are injured. At noon on the 19th, a pregnant woman surnamed Su, living in the Iron Buddha Temple in Nanguan, came to exchange a one-yuan Gongyu paper money and was knocked down and trampled, fainting. Neighbors rushed to her rescue and poured her with goat's blood before she woke up. However, because she was six months pregnant, her injuries were particularly severe, and she was reported to be in critical condition this morning. Public opinion is in an uproar and has to blame the authorities for their inappropriate measures. They have questioned the Chamber of Commerce. The President of the Chamber of Commerce, Lan Bohua, feeling unfairly blamed on behalf of the money merchants, decided to ask the county government to stop the public exchange and let each money house exchange separately to avoid people gathering and causing another tragedy. This afternoon, the reporter personally went to inspect. It was during the break, and the double doors were tightly closed. Armed military police were patrolling the Chamber of Commerce courtyard with guns. The door was surrounded by wooden fences, and people were shoulder to shoulder and heel to heel in the fences, and some were standing on the wooden fences and on people's shoulders. An old woman surnamed Wang, living on Yunlong Mountain, was squeezed into the wooden fence and was about to faint. She was helped out. The Director of the Telegraph Bureau, Kuang Jingyou, happened to meet her during a visit. Seeing that she was holding a one-yuan Gongyu paper money, Kuang generously paid her two yuan of钞幣 (钞幣) and took the Gongyu paper money, tore it up, and threw it away. The onlookers shouted admiration. Kuang also bought her a car to send her home, otherwise, another tragedy would have occurred. At the moment, society expresses great sympathy for the pregnant woman who was trampled and is in critical condition. They have decided that if the woman unfortunately dies, they will form a Support Association for the Tragedy to demand compensation from the paper merchants. Public sentiment is激昻 (激昻), which is可徽 (可徽). (Twentieth)

Suzhou: Jiangsu Province Water Police Implements Downsizing

The Department of Civil Affairs is implementing downsizing to reorganize the provincial water police, eliminating the weak and retaining the strong. It has now been decided to change the six major districts into four districts. The first district of Minhang remains the same, with Xu Pucheng as the district chief. The second district of Wuxi and Suzhou are merged into the second district, with the district headquarters located in Suzhou and Wei Zhanyuan as the district chief. The fourth district of Wusong is changed to the third district, with Chi Yaozong as the district chief. The fifth district of Guazhou and the sixth district of Qingjiangpu are merged into the fourth district, with the district headquarters located in Guazhou and Gong Guoliang as the district chief. Each district is divided into four major teams, and each major team has three sub-teams. Each sub-team has three patrol boats and one large boat, which is almost half of the original number. The district headquarters also has a special task force with 60 team members and an investigation team with one team leader, two team members, and thirteen investigators. The above methods were decided by the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Gu Renfa, at a meeting of district chiefs convened in the province. The second district chief, Wei Zhanyuan, returned to Suzhou on the 21st, bringing with him 500 yuan in silver for paying arrears and severance pay. Because the district has a vast territory, governing Changshu, Kunshan, Wujiang, Wuxian, Piaoyang, Wuxi, Wujin, Yixing, and other eight counties, it is necessary to establish six major teams. The original police force of the second and third districts was more than 2,000. During the downsizing, about 1,000 people were retained and formed into five major teams. Another guerrilla team was编充 (编充) into one major team. The downsizing must be implemented by the end of this month. At that time, Director Gu will personally depart to each district for point編 (編).

Wuxi: Shanghai Parricide Captured in Wuxi

Zhou Chen, a widow from Yancheng, residing at No. 66, Guangzhao Road, Zhabei, Shanghai, next to the Guangdong Guild Hall, is about 40 years old. Having no children, she relies on her late husband's inheritance to collect usury and live. Her husband's elder brother, Zhang Qing, had a son named Tongjiang (also known as Xiao Erzi), who is over 20 years old. Because he coveted Chen's late husband's inheritance, he once litigated in court. As a result, Zhang Qing lost the lawsuit. Therefore, Zhang Qing and his son both hated Chen. The following year, Zhang Qing also passed away, and Tongjiang planned and premeditated, harboring deep resentment towards Chen, eventually leading to a潜伏杀机 (潜伏杀机). At about 4:00 PM on August 4th of this year, while Zhou Chen was washing filthy utensils by the nearby river, he held a kitchen knife and砍 (砍) her face and abdomen three times, causing her to bleed profusely and barely breathe. Tongjiang, seeing that his goal had been achieved,揚長而逸 (揚長而逸). The Second Division of the Fourth District of the Public Security Bureau of the管辖 (管辖) area派 (派) police to send the injured to the hospital. Due to the severity of the injuries, she died shortly after. The Shanghai District Court Procurator personally came to騐收殮 (騐收殮) and ordered the arrest of the murderer, but to no avail. Recently, Chen's younger brother, Xue Shi, learned that Tongjiang was hiding in this county. He immediately came to Wuxi to search for him. The day before yesterday (20th) afternoon, he caught a glimpse of Tongjiang watching a play at the Zhenxing Theater on Dongxin Road. He remained silent, left the theater, and reported to the Water Patrol Team Leader Qian Tianzhui. Team Leader Qian personally led the police to the theater and拘獲 (拘獲) Zhou Tongjiang (also known as Xiao Sanzi) and brought him back to the team. Yesterday, he presented him to the county government for questioning and押 (押) him, awaiting the Shanghai District Court to come to Wuxi to提 (提) him.

Letter: Letter from Zhenjiang District Court

To the Editor: Reading your newspaper's report on the 18th of this month about prisoners in Zhenjiang Court going on a hunger strike, it stated that prisoner Xia Yisong suddenly went mad, with excessive nerve刺激 (刺激), and after medical diagnosis, his condition was severe, and there was a danger to his life. Repeated requests were made to transfer him to the hospital for treatment, but the court had no specific measures. All官犯 (官犯) in detention went on a hunger strike from the 16th to request, etc. After investigation, although the warden of the prison reported that prisoner Xia Yisong was indeed ill, the director of the Department of Internal Medicine of the Jiangsu Provincial Hospital was immediately ordered to conduct three diagnoses. His body temperature was 37 degrees Celsius, his pulse was 84 beats per minute, his上下 (上下) was still neat, his breathing was quiet, not喘急 (喘急), and his pupil response was normal. There were no abnormalities in the lungs or heart, and no abnormalities in the abdomen. According to the doctor's diagnosis results, Xia Yisong's condition was not a danger to his life, and it was not that he was not paying attention to the prisoners at all. Other prisoners did not go on a hunger strike either. In fact, the above report does not conform to the truth and should be corrected. To Shenbao Newspaper, from the Prosecutor's Office of Jiangsu Zhenjiang District Court, November 20th.
