Local News: News from Various Sides After the Fujian Incident; Content of the 民衆 (民衆) Representative Assembly's Clever Telegram; Advice to Chiang and Cai from the No War Association's Ma Telegram; Fujian Groups Telegraphing to Request Maintenance of the Status Quo

The Far East News Agency reports that the Fujian Provincial Rebellion has now become a reality, and the People's Government it organized was formally established last month. The Far East News Agency reporter yesterday learned from various sources the details of what happened before and after. The information obtained is recorded as follows:

People's Representative Assembly

According to sources, Chen (Mingshu) and Cai (Tingkai) and others have been planning the organization of the new government for a long time. Chen Mingshu's travels between Hong Kong and Fujian were specifically for contacting various parties. After the plan was finalized, he hastily returned to Fujian and incited his subordinates on the morning of the 18th to hold a "National People's Representative Assembly" in Zhangzhou, and resolved to ask Chen, Cai, Li (Jishen), and others to come forward to organize a "People's Government" in the name of the Assembly, and determined that Zhangzhou would be the temporary capital of the government. It is said in the newspaper that the government was established in Fuzhou, which is actually a misreport.

Main Idea of the Clever Telegram's Content

On the same day, a clever telegram was also issued in the name of the Assembly. The telegram was telegraphed by the telegraph bureau and printed on oil-paper and sent from other sources. The Min people traveling in Shanghai received a copy of the eight-hundred-word telegram on the previous night (20th). The telegram still advertised both the resistance to Japan and suppression of bandits.

Re-Issuing the Establishment Telegram

Chen and others had accepted the request of the People's Representative Assembly on the 18th. Everything was prepared beforehand, so there was no need to exaggerate. They convened a citizens' meeting in Zhangzhou on the morning of the 20th and announced the establishment of the "People's Government." The establishment telegram was sent on the same day. The Nanjing Central Government received the telegram the day before yesterday, and the Shanghai Municipal Government also received it at the same time, but Mayor Wu told reporters that he had not yet received it.

Saying That Jiang Guangnai Was Detained

A bizarre rumor was prevalent in the city yesterday, saying that Jiang Guangnai was detained by Chen Mingshu and others. The newspapers had previously reported that the Fujian affairs were actively planned by Chen, Jiang, and Cai. However, when the news of the government's establishment came out, Jiang's name was not included in the organization, which inevitably raised suspicions. Therefore, it was rumored that Jiang had been detained. However, according to the reporter's investigation from another source, this is actually the talk of a nervous person. In fact, Jiang temporarily hid his name due to some relationship.

Central Government Temporarily Not Sending Troops

As for the Central Government's response to the Fujian affairs, it issued a telegram to the whole country the day before yesterday, ordering all military and political organs to quickly handle them. However, it is learned that the Central Government has always advocated resolving any previous incidents politically and will never lightly use force, causing suffering to the people. Therefore, in this Fujian incident, it still intends to send personnel to疏解 (疏解) and will not meet with soldiers for the time being.

Attitude of Central Committee Members Staying in Shanghai

The reporter yesterday visited Li Liejun, He Shizhen, Sun Jingya, Gui Chongji, and other members of the Central Committee staying in Shanghai and asked them about their attitude towards the Fujian affairs. They all said that none of them had seen the telegram issued by the Fujian side, so they did not fully understand the truth of the Fujian affairs. Before the truth is clear, it is not convenient to express their attitude. They may have something to say in two or three days. As for Madame Chen Bijun, the wife of the President of the Executive Yuan, Wang Jingwei, she arrived in Shanghai by overnight express train from Beijing at about 7:00 AM yesterday. It was reported that Madame Wang came here to visit the members of the Central Committee staying in Shanghai to inquire about their attitude towards the Fujian affairs. However, He, Sun, Gui, and others said when they met with reporters that Madame Wang had not come to visit. Later, the reporter met Madame Wang at Chu Minyi's private residence. Madame Wang only said "I don't know," likely denying the matter.

Japan Sends Warships to Fujian

After the Fujian incident occurred, Japan attached great importance to it. Under the pretext of protecting overseas Chinese, it will send six destroyers from Magong Port to Fuzhou and Xiamen to observe.

The New Voice News Agency said that after the Fujian Rebellion was confirmed, the Central Government decided to take severe measures. However, Central Committee member Chen Bijun came to Shanghai to contact the Central Committee members and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. Details are recorded below:

When the Central Political Committee met the day before yesterday, the members of the Central Committee pushed Central Committee member Chen Bijun to come to Shanghai to contact the Central Committee members staying in Shanghai to deal with the Fujian incident. Chen took the night train from Beijing that night and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning.

No War Association Sends Ma Telegram

Since the news of the Fujian Rebellion arrived in Shanghai, the Abolish Civil War League convened a meeting of the standing committee to discuss it. Yesterday afternoon, it sent a telegram advising Chiang and Cai: "Fuzhou Chairman Chiang and Director Cai, Upon receiving the news of the变讯 (变讯), we were shocked. You once made a statement in Shanghai that you would not participate in the civil war. The words are still in our ears, how can you forget your heart? How can we bear to鬩牆 (鬩牆) in this situation? We dare to ask you to turn back before it is too late, store up strength, and use it against foreign forces. We dare to offer忠告 (忠告). We hope you will adopt it. The Abolish Civil War League Headquarters respectfully, Ma."

Chen Zhaoying Has Returned to Beijing

Before the Fujian Rebellion occurred, the Central Government had decided to send Chen Zhaoying and Duan Xipeng to Fujian to investigate and疏解 (疏解). After Chen came to Shanghai the day before yesterday, he was about to prepare to go, but learned that the政变 (政变) had been confirmed and that going would be useless, so he stopped going. He returned to Beijing the night before last. As for Duan Xipeng, he never left Beijing.

Shanghai-Fujian Telegrams Are Open

Telegrams between Shanghai and Fujian were interrupted on the evening of the 19th due to the construction of roads and bombing of mountains, which damaged the报線 (报線). Yesterday morning, the报線 (报線) between Jiangshan and Pucheng was repaired. From 10:44 AM, the报機 (报機) connecting to Fuzhou was open and could receive and send telegrams as usual. However, due to strict inspection, the delivery of telegrams is not as fast as before. The China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong route also flew south as usual yesterday morning. The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau did not receive orders to stop remittance transactions to Fuzhou, Xiamen, and other places, and continued to handle them as usual. The China News Agency said that Li Jishen, Chen Mingshu, and others in Fujian Province established a separate People's Government, and its telegram was issued on the 20th. The Central Bank's branches in Fuzhou and Xiamen have been taken over by the Fujian side. The naval organizations in Fujian are particularly numerous. The marines stationed in Mawei were disarmed on the 18th. Other state-run transportation and tax revenue organizations are now under the surveillance of the Fujian army. Yesterday, the reporter inquired about the details from various parties and summarized them as follows:

Central Bank Notes Can Only Be Used to Pay Taxes

Since the pacification director Cai Tingcuo sent Li Chaoheng and Ye Shaoquan to take over and reorganize the Fuzhou and Xiamen branches of the Central Bank and temporarily suspend business, all Central Bank paper money can no longer circulate in Fujian Province. According to reliable news obtained by the banking sector in Shanghai yesterday, all Central Bank paper money in Fujian Province can only be used to pay national and local taxes, and cannot be circulated in any other way.

Two Naval Vessels Stationed in Fujian

There are many naval organizations in Fujian, such as the marines, the naval training camp, the Changmen Fortress, the Xiamen Naval Aviation Office, the Majiang Naval Academy, and the Mawei and Xiamen naval shipyards. Except for the marines stationed in Zhangzhou, Xiamen, Quanzhou, Mindu, and Mawei, the others have fixed locations. The reporter learned the news after the Fujian Rebellion from the naval side in Shanghai yesterday. According to them, the Majiang marines were taken over by the 19th Route Army on the 18th with 2,000 troops. However, the marines stationed there only numbered twenty or thirty, so they were handed over immediately without any incidents. However, the majority of the marines are stationed in Sandu. As for the Xiamen Aviation Office, there are currently about six or seven airplanes, as well as the Changmen Fortress and naval shipyards. As of yesterday, no one had gone to take them over, so Chen Wenlin, the director of the Aviation Office who came to Shanghai, flew back to Xiamen yesterday. Currently, there are only two small warships, Hai Fu and Hai Ning, stationed in Majiang and Xiamen. As for whether the Ministry of Navy needs to send ships there, it is said that it must wait for orders from the Central Government and is not yet necessary. Rumors that Japanese warships are sailing to Fujian and will take action are not credible. In short, the intention is to show off power under the pretext of protecting overseas Chinese. Commander Chen Jiliang went to Beijing and has not returned as of yesterday. All Central Government tax revenue agencies in Fujian have been in the hands of the Fujian government since the 19th. The naval coastal radio station established by the Fujian People's Government in Wusong received a telegram yesterday and forwarded it to the Gaochang Temple Headquarters. The content mentioned resisting Japan and suppressing Communists, but the original text was not seen.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Ships Not Detained

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is a state-run transportation organization. It has a branch office in Fuzhou and an agency in Xiamen. The reporter feared that the Fujian side would detain ships, so he specifically met with Chen Weiqing, the general affairs section chief of the company. According to him, only the Taishun ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is sailing to Fujian. It is currently en route and is expected to arrive in Shanghai tomorrow. It is true that the Central Bank's branch offices in Fujian have been taken over, but there is no definite news about the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's branch office. The director of the Fujian branch office came to Shanghai the day before yesterday and has now transferred to Hangzhou, so everything will be known after the branch office returns. In short, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's property in Fujian only includes a few branch office buildings, land, vacant land, four warehouses, and docks, which are few in number. Whether航輪 (航輪) will call at Fujian and Xiamen again in the future is still under consideration by the company. However, as of now, none of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's航輪 (航輪) have been detained by the Fujian side.

Shanghai-Guangdong Airplanes As Usual

The China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong route has just been completed. The entire route has seven stops, and Fuzhou and Xiamen are both landing stops. After the sudden change in the Fujian situation, the company, being a commercial civilian aviation organization, is entirely for business purposes. Therefore, according to a staff member in the company yesterday, the Fujian affairs have no impact on the Shanghai-Guangdong route. The flight from Shanghai to Guangdong yesterday morning still took off as usual at 6:05 AM and landed at the Fuzhou and Xiamen stops as usual. The flight from Guangdong to Shanghai will arrive in Shanghai today.

The Impact of Shanghai-Fujian Commerce

Yesterday, a reporter from Xinxin News Agency specially inquired with a person in charge of a Fujian merchant in Shanghai about the recent commercial situation between Shanghai and Fujian. According to the person, the loss suffered by Fujian merchants in Shanghai after the changes in the Fujian situation was quite large. This is because many Shanghai merchants have been remitting funds to Fujian Province to purchase goods in recent days. Unexpectedly, with a sudden change in the political situation, the purchased goods were mostly blocked due to transportation issues and could not be shipped to Shanghai. They will have to wait for the political situation to stabilize before shipping can resume. However, the funds for purchasing goods have already been remitted, and the goods cannot arrive as scheduled. The significant impact on their economy can be imagined. The reporter also learned from another source that after the political changes in Fujian, the commercial transactions between Shanghai and Fujian, up to yesterday, included both Fujian merchants wiring to Shanghai to continue purchasing goods and wiring to stop shipment. This shows one aspect of the chaotic commercial situation in the province. If the political situation does not develop further, the shipping between Shanghai and Fujian is likely to be interrupted.

Overseas Chinese Stop Going to Fujian

According to Xinxin News Agency, five overseas Chinese from Southeast Asia, including Li Shuanghui, Li Tiemin, He Baoren, Huang Xiaoyan, and Liu Weiming, were originally scheduled to take the Jiesheng Wheel from Shanghai to Fujian yesterday to investigate the political, economic, educational, and social conditions of the province. They also planned to meet with Jiang Guangnai, Cai Tingkai, Chen Mingshu, etc., to contribute their opinions on Fujian affairs as private individuals, hoping for realization. Unexpectedly, the situation in Fujian has worsened, so the delegation decided to change its itinerary and will stop going to Fujian. They plan to stay in Shanghai for a while and then return directly to Singapore. It is also learned that Li Shuanghui, a representative of the delegation and a veteran of overseas Chinese in our country, took an early train from Shanghai to Beijing yesterday morning to pay a visit to Executive Yuan President Wang and Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee Chairman Chen Shuren for some matters.

Central Factory Inspection Office Sends Cheng Haifeng to Shanghai to Investigate Major Factories Starting Today

Since the establishment of the Central Factory Inspection Office, various inspection plans have been actively drafted. Recently, in order to understand the factory conditions in various developed industrial areas so that they can be used as references when drafting various plans, Inspection Section Chief Cheng Haifeng was specially sent to Shanghai. Cheng arrived in Shanghai on the 20th and immediately went to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to meet with Tian Heqing, the director of the Factory Inspection Section, to cooperate in the investigation. According to Tian Heqing's statement to the Central News Agency reporter, Cheng will be accompanied by personnel from the bureau starting today to visit larger factories, staying for about three or four days, and then going to Hangzhou, Wuxi, Qingdao, Tianjin, Hankou, and other places. Two Railways Pay Interest on Loans

The two batches of loans that expired on May 18 of last year for the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and on the 17th of this month for the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, totaling £116,000 in principal for the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and £37,593 15s in principal for the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, have now been decided to pay interest first. The Beijing-Shanghai Railway's interest, including bank commission, totals £69,774, equivalent to $1,076,032.77 in national currency. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway's interest, including bank commission, totals £11,278 2s 6d, equivalent to $170,927.71 in national currency. The total of $1,249,960.48 in national currency has already been withdrawn and allocated from the special reserve fund on November 6.

Mr. Bissell Talks About Sino-Philippine International Aviation Not Being Stopped Due to Obstruction by the Philippine Parliament

The Shanghai Times reported that Mr. Bissell, the American director of China National Aviation Corporation, who recently went to the Philippines on behalf of Pacific American Airways, a subsidiary of United Aircraft and Transport Corporation, to negotiate air routes, returned to Shanghai by plane from Guangzhou on Sunday. Yesterday (20th), he stated that the Philippine Legislative Assembly's refusal to grant Pacific American Airways the franchise for internal aviation on the island is not enough to hinder Pacific American Airways' Sino-Philippine international aviation plan. Approximately as soon as suitable aircraft are built, passengers can travel from Hong Kong to Manila. As for the Philippine Parliament's rejection of the franchise proposal, it is because they fear that the already established small companies in the Philippines will be oppressed after Pacific American Airways joins the internal aviation business on the island. Therefore, we can still fly from Hong Kong to Manila and land in Northern Luzon to refuel. It is anticipated that the Philippine Legislative Assembly's refusal to allow the company to open additional branch routes within the Philippine Islands will not have a significant impact.

In addition, it is also heard that the test flight results of the Shanghai-Hong Kong-Guangzhou air route organized by China National Aviation Corporation are very satisfactory. Approximately within the next week, passenger service can begin. As for when air service between Hong Kong and Manila can be started, Mr. Bissell did not give a definite answer, only saying that it is expected that it will take at least one year to build suitable facilities in the United States.

Chairman Chiang's Reply to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Telegram: Suppressing Bandits is the Natural Duty of the Military and People

Chiang Chung-cheng."

Page 11

Preparing to Organize a National Grain Production and Sales Organization; Preparatory Meeting to be Held in Shanghai on the 6th of Next Month

According to the Dagong News, when Chairman Chiang Kai-shek convened a grain meeting of eight provinces and cities, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hunan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Hubei, and Shanghai, in Jiangxi, representatives from Shanghai, Wu Huanru, Gu Xinyi, etc., suggested organizing a grain production and sales cooperative organization to regulate national food supply and prevent the dumping of foreign rice. After the proposal was passed by the entire body, the representatives from Shanghai were appointed to be responsible for planning the organizational outline and capital budget of the production and sales organization. After the plans were drafted, they were jointly submitted to Chairman Chiang for review and approval. Therefore, it was decided to convene representatives from various provinces and cities in Shanghai on December 6 to hold the first preparatory meeting. The details are recorded below.

Chairman Chiang's Directive

Gu Xinyi, chairman of the Shanghai Soybean and Rice Trade Association, and others received a directive from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's headquarters yesterday, which stated: "Your submitted document, regarding the draft outline of the grain production and sales cooperation method and the proposed Article 2, regarding how to borrow and allocate the one million yuan allocated by the government, is hereby requested for review and instruction, is hereby acknowledged. The submitted document and the outline of the method have been noted. The seven articles of the draft outline of the grain production and sales cooperation method, with one million yuan to be raised by commercial firms in various places and one million yuan to be borrowed from the government with interest, are generally feasible, and it is stipulated that the one million yuan allocated by the Central Government shall be guaranteed principal and interest by the commercial party, which can be approved. You should immediately follow the outline of the method, stipulate the various items, and organize them in a practical manner, and quickly collect the one million yuan in commercial shares and report it to this headquarters for responsible application. Government banks should borrow or overdraft the full amount at interest to facilitate coordination. The outline of the method is kept for reference. This order."

Convening the First Meeting

Yesterday, the representatives from Shanghai sent telegrams to the representatives from various provinces, which stated: "Regarding the preparation for the establishment of a grain production and sales cooperative organization, the outline of the method has been submitted to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's headquarters in Nanchang for review and approval (the directive is as mentioned above). It has been decided to hold the first preparatory meeting in Shanghai on December 6. We sincerely hope that your representative will come to Shanghai to attend the meeting and jointly discuss the progress. We hereby send this letter and hope that you will reply in advance. Respectfully, (Guangdong) Wen Zhongqi, (Zhejiang) Wang Zhengying, (Hubei) Jia Shiyi, Jiang Han Luo, (Hebei) Shi Jinghuan, Ji Hua, (Hunan) Zhang Kailian, Tan Changkai, (Jiangsu) Dong Guangfu, Tong Yumin, (Anhui) Yuan Fen, (Henan) Xu Daochun, (Jiangxi) Zhu Huaibing, Gong Wensui."

Internal Content of the Organizational Method

According to Gu Xinyi, chairman of the Soybean and Rice Trade Association, speaking to a Dagong News reporter, the organization of the grain production and sales cooperation organization is as follows: (1) Each province will send one representative to establish a board of directors, and a manager will be mutually elected from the directors to handle all matters; (2) Each provincial and municipal government will send one representative to establish a supervisory board to supervise the affairs of the board of directors; (3) The head office will be located in Shanghai, and branch offices will not be established in other provinces. The head office will directly send personnel to contact the purchase and sale of grain in various places; (4) The capital for grain production and sales will total 10 million yuan, with 2 million yuan as working capital and 8 million yuan as bank collateralized working capital; (5) It will be named the China Grain Transportation and Marketing Company, and the draft articles of association will be drafted in accordance with the Limited Company Organization Law.

Production, Sales, and Transportation Methods

Six provinces, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, are the national rice-producing regions. South China's Guangdong, Fujian, North China's Tianjin, and Beiping are all non-rice-producing regions. However, Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have dense populations, and the grain produced each year can only supply consumption within the province. Anhui, Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces have the most abundant production, but because transportation is difficult and supply and demand are uneven, Fujian and Guangdong provinces use foreign rice. The previous eight-province grain meeting discussed this in detail, and Chairman Chiang was responsible for suggesting that the government order the national railways and China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and other land and water transportation to reduce freight rates and other miscellaneous fees for grain.

Ministry Order to Facilitate Grain Transportation

In order to increase rice prices and relieve rural areas, the Ministry of Railways sent a telegram to the two railways, which stated: "The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus have read the micro-telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's headquarters in Nanchang, which stated that the most important principle of the grain meeting's resolution to increase rice prices and relieve rural areas is to eliminate obstacles, facilitate transportation, reduce grain transportation prices, and promote sales. It is hereby telegraphed to you that whenever a request to transport rice is received, you must give priority to allocating vehicles, reducing transportation procedures, in order to ensure smooth grain transportation, increase rice prices, and achieve the effect of relieving rural areas. You must comply with this. Minister Gu Mengyu, printed."

Liu Hongsheng Reports on China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Affairs, With Slight Differences From Yesterday's Newspaper

The General Manager of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent a letter to this newspaper, which stated: "To the gentlemen of the editorial department, I am writing respectfully. Today, your newspaper published an article entitled "Liu Hongsheng Reports That the Future of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is Optimistic," which stated that commemorative weeks were held, employees were notified to gather at the bureau, and the Economic Committee decided to allocate a large amount of money to repay the old debt of HSBC first. These statements are not in accordance with what I said. Even when I am unable to attend the commemorative week due to reasons, the employees also participate as a whole. I did not know about the gathering. The news reported is not entirely accurate. Please correct it in a prominent place based on this letter. I am grateful for your assistance. Respectfully, Liu Hongsheng."

All demands will be discussed further after resuming work. The Municipal Federation of Trade Unions also issued a statement to all walks of life. The details are recorded below.

Union's Notice of Resumption of Work

The Strike Committee of the Water and Electricity Industry Union of the Fourth District issued a notice of resumption of work yesterday, which stated: "Regarding the notice, this time, all comrades of our union, in accordance with legal procedures, went through running around and negotiation to conduct a slowdown strike warning in order to demand the consolidation of the guarantee of deserved rights. Due to the slowdown strike warning, they were forced to strike, which lasted for nearly two months. During these nearly two months, the spirit of hardship of all comrades has not been sympathized with by the company authorities. However, enthusiastic social leaders and the Chinese directors and the president and chief inspector in charge of municipal affairs have fully recognized that all comrades of our union are elements who have a strong sense of reason, who love public safety and overcome anger, and that the rights fought for by all comrades of our union are indeed created by previous labor and have been recognized and promised by the Bureau of Works and the American Foreign Power Company that took over the Electric Power Company. The facts have also been announced to society. The debate on right and wrong is extremely clear. Therefore, it is now decided, on November 22, under the advice of leaders such as Du Yuesheng, Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Ludeng, Xu Xinliu, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Kui Yanfang, and Cai Futang, to resume work with pain in order to safeguard social public safety and public interests. Regarding the method of guaranteeing deserved rights, we will quietly wait for the enthusiastic mediating Chinese directors and leaders to properly discuss it again after the resumption of work. Therefore, this notice is issued to all comrades to follow it consistently. It is greatly hoped."

Issuing a Declaration of Resuming Work

The Water and Electricity Industry Union of the Fourth District issued a declaration of resuming work with pain, which stated: "Since our electrical workers' union was forced to conduct a slowdown strike, it has been 54 days. All our workers deeply know the importance of the electrical industry to social security, and we have always sought a solution through proper channels, and we have never dared to overstep the boundaries and affect social order. Past facts should be recognized by people from all walks of life. Now, the company authorities, urged by public opinion, and with the mediation of Du Yuesheng, Yu Qiaqing, Xu Xinliu, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Kui Yanfang, and other gentlemen, have begun negotiations and decided on the prerequisites for resuming work. Although this method is not as expected by everyone, the sincerity of the gentlemen's enthusiastic mediation is enough to make people grateful and weep. In order to accept the mediator's intentions and safeguard public safety, it has been decided to resume work with pain this morning. In addition to representing all workers in expressing thanks to people from all walks of life and to gentlemen such as Du, Yu, Xu, Wang, Lin, and Kui, we will make efforts in the future with the original intention of serving the community. I hereby announce a few words, hoping for your understanding."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits a Request to the Municipal Government to Return

The Wartime Advances of Jiangwan Businessmen

Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Municipal Government, which stated: "Regarding the submission of a request based on the facts, on the 18th of this month, a letter from the Jiangwan Branch Office of the affiliated association stated that during the January 28th Incident, this office, together with party and government agencies and various groups, organized the Jiangwan Temporary Security Committee to facilitate supply and maintain security. At that time, we borrowed and advanced funds from various businesses for application, totaling $3,494.96. This was registered with the Municipal Government by the municipal commissioner of this district in March of last year, requesting allocation and return. Later, we received instructions, roughly stating that we should wait for the summary of the case and forward it to the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs for verification. However, two years have passed, and there is no news. Various businesses have been coming to the office to urge the return of the advances, which is very difficult to answer. Therefore, in September of this year, we received a letter from the office of the municipal commissioner of this district, convening the relevant agencies and groups to open a meeting and decide on three measures, which were also submitted to the Municipal Government for review. Unexpectedly, two months have passed, and there has been no approval. At this time, the end of the year is approaching, and the disasters are after the calamity. The meeting of merchants and markets is sluggish. The expectations of the various businesses for the return of the advances are like hunger and thirst. If proper plans are not made, it will be impossible to respond if something happens in the future, and the fundraising of other donations and leases will be even more difficult to start. We have specially prepared a document to apply, hoping that you will forward it to the Municipal Government for assistance. If it can be returned as soon as possible, the business difficulties can be relieved, and the reputation can be maintained, which will not only be the fortune of the local area. Upon arrival, it was found that this advance was purely for maintaining local security during wartime. At that time, the business community raised this amount for the official, which was no different from ordinary debt. After the situation stabilized, there would eventually be a day of repayment. Two years have passed, and there is still no news of debt repayment. The feeling of anxiety is naturally unavoidable. The three repayment methods discussed are indeed a last resort to seek this remedy in order to alleviate the urgency of self. It is reasonable to record the three original resolutions and submit them to your office for adoption and implementation. A quick approval will be a public convenience."

Heze County Telegraphed to Request Continued Winter Relief

Due to the severe floods in Heze, Shandong, the Chinese Relief Society, together with the Yellow River Flood Relief Association, raised 70,000 yuan, 5,000 sets of cotton clothing, and a large number of medicines, etc., and publicly appointed Li Yunmen to carry out the relief efforts. However, there are more than 100,000 flood victims in the area, and the funds are insufficient to provide relief to all of them. The association recently received a telegram from Qin Jian, etc., of the Heze County Flood Relief Association, stating that the relief funds, cotton clothing, medicines, etc., donated by your association were distributed impartially by Li Yunmen, who did not spare any effort, and the flood victims shared the benefits and were deeply grateful. However, as the winter season is approaching, relief is urgently needed. We earnestly request the continued issuance of benevolent aid to expand the scope of salvation, and we also request Li Yunmen to continue to handle the matter to make use of his experience. We are immensely grateful, etc. After receiving the telegram, the association deeply understood the difficult situation of the flood victims in Heze, but was unable to provide further assistance due to financial exhaustion. It is found that natural disasters and man-made calamities have occurred in our country in recent years, without any place being spared, and they are becoming increasingly severe. The ancient saying "mournful cries of the displaced are heard everywhere" is being seen today. How can everyone develop a compassionate and grand wish, economize on food and clothing, and deliberate for the lives of the flood victims to save our compatriots from deep waters and scorching fires?

Wang Shengrong Dies From Serious Injuries; Two Gangsters Escorted to Court for Interrogation; Police Lawyer States the Circumstances of the Shooting; Many Accomplices Still at Large and Not Captured

Wang Shengrong, a gangster from Ningbo, 23 years old, lived with his concubine, Fu Genjin (also known as Ah Liu) from Suzhou, in the rear building of No. 1 Chongshanfang, Dengtuo Road. They specialized in armed gangs going out to rob, and Fu was in charge of smuggling firearms. They committed many crimes. In the morning, Chinese detective Ke Zhang of the Huishi Police Department learned of Wang's whereabouts and reported to the head of the detective team. Together with Chinese Detective Chief Shao Jingfan, Detective Liang Yuliang, Western Detective Latuo, and Mitde, they broke down the door and entered the address. Because Wang attempted to resist, he was shot by the Western Detective.

Shooting Injury

Wang and Fu were apprehended on the spot, and a handgun with twenty-two bullets was seized. A fellow accomplice, Zhu Liangfa, from Ningbo, was subsequently captured. They were taken to the police station. Except for Wang Shengrong, who was sent to the Public Works Department Hospital due to his injuries, the rest were detained separately. These details were previously reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Wang Shengrong's injuries were critical, and despite medical treatment, he died at 11 p.m. that evening. The hospital notified the police station, and the body was transported to the mortuary on Avenue Foch for examination. Yesterday morning, the thief, Fu Gengjin, and Zhu Liangfa were sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court, requesting permission for their detention for further investigation. According to police station lawyer Wang Yaotang, at 6:55 a.m. yesterday, the police station received information that

Bandits Hideout

bandits were hiding in the back room of No. 1 Chongshan Fang, Dengtu Road. Chinese and foreign detectives went to arrest them. Upon entering the room, they saw two people lying under a quilt. The detectives drew their guns and ordered them not to move. However, the man lying on the outer bed suddenly reached under his pillow as if to grab something. The detectives ordered him to stop, but he did not comply. Fearing an accident, for self-defense, the foreign detective, Latour, fired one shot. However, he did not stop his movement. He then fired two more shots. At the same time, the detective stepped forward and pulled back the quilt, revealing a man and a woman (Wang Shengrong and Fu Gengjin). They were immediately arrested. Wang was shot twice, once in the chest and once in the arm, and was bleeding profusely. Under the pillow, they found

Live Ammunition Handgun

a handgun containing six bullets. Under the bedding, they found four and a half ounces of red pills. In the drawer, they found sixteen bullets. A moment later, an old woman rushed in and was also arrested at the time. She was also taken to the police station. Except for Wang, who was sent to the hospital for treatment, it was learned that the old woman was Wang's mother, named Wang Zhao, who came to see her son after hearing the news. Since she was not involved, she was released. As for the defendant, Zhu Liangfa, he went to Wang's place to borrow money at 11 a.m. and was detained by the stationed detectives. According to Zhu's statement at the police station, he went to Wang's place yesterday to borrow money. However, Fu Gengjin proved that Zhu had also

Participated in Robbery

and received a share of silver dollars, so he was detained. Later, the detectives went to the hospital to question the injured thief, Wang Shengrong. According to Wang, the handgun belonged to Yan Chunfu, who was on the run. Yan lived at No. 48, Lane 912, East-West Huade Road. When detectives went to investigate, Yan had already moved elsewhere around 8 a.m. When the Shanghai Moving Company's report was found, it was learned that Yan had moved to No. 180, Tangshan Road. However, when they arrived at Tangshan Road, the furniture was there, but Yan was nowhere to be found and could not be arrested. It is believed that he had

Fled Upon Hearing the News

It has been verified that the handgun seized in this case was used within the past week, but the specific case has not yet been determined. Furthermore, accomplices Chen Xinggui and Zhu Mapi are still at large. Therefore, a request has been made for permission to detain them. In her interrogation, Fu Gengjin confessed that she met Wang during the Shanghai war and lived with him at No. 1 Chongshan Fang. Wang was unemployed. Around September of last year, she went to Chen Xinggui's place at Room 12 of the Central Hotel in Xiaodongmen and obtained the handgun, which she brought back and gave to Wang. Until March or April of this year, she twice saw Wang and Yan Chunfu leave together and return several hours later, carrying

Fur Coats and Clothing

When I asked them where the clothes came from, they said, "You wouldn't understand. We took them from the road." She knew nothing else. As for Zhu Lianggui, she saw Wang give him five dollars and also give him clothes to pawn. When questioned, Zhu denied being a thief. Judge Xue Lanru examined the confessions and ordered that Fu and Zhu be detained for seven days for further investigation. Meanwhile, the prosecutor's office of the Special Court appointed prosecutor Diao Chengtang to inspect the mortuary and examine Wang Shengrong's body. After ascending the court, he questioned Fu Gengjin briefly and ruled that the deceased, Wang Shengrong, died from a gunshot wound to the chest sustained while still alive. The body was handed over to Pushan Villa for burial.

Detectives in Disguise Bust a Gambling Den in Pudong, Arresting Eleven Gambling and Drug Offenders; Gambling Paraphernalia and Opium Pipes Confiscated for Investigation

Sha Jinggui, a well-known gangster from Pudong, 28 years old, from Chongming, started a gambling den in February of this year by colluding with local gamblers such as Gu Zhengquan. It was located inside No. 29, Qiu Family Wooden Bridge, east of Yangjing Town, Pudong. It served as a gambling venue and a "swallows' nest." The front of the house was used for gambling games such as dice, pai gow, poker, and mahjong, attracting ignorant men and women to gamble all night long and profiting by skimming. The back of the house was an opium den and a red pill den, providing addicts with their fix. The gambling venue had snack stalls, fruit stalls, tea and wheat stalls, and small wine shops on both sides, on a large scale with all kinds of gambling equipment available. At night, the lights shone brightly, making it look like a painting. The nearby residents all regarded the place as a trap. Recently, disputes arose among the gamblers over the distribution of loot, causing disturbances. Detectives Shen Wenda and Qiu Shuxian of the City Public Security Bureau's Detective Team learned about it and reported the information to Captain Lu Ying, who in turn reported it to Director Wen Hongen. Wen, upon receiving the report, immediately issued an order instructing Captain Lu to send a large number of detectives, including Detective Foremen Chen Guangyan and Li Xiaobao, and Ling Tianpeng, along with six police officers from the bureau's Police Brigade, all in disguise. At around 11 p.m. the night before, they secretly crossed the river to the gambling den at No. 29, Qiu Family Wooden Bridge, east of Yangjing Town, Pudong, and surrounded it. The detectives disguised themselves as gamblers and successively infiltrated the gambling den. The gamblers at each table were shouting and cheering excitedly. They suddenly shouted, "Grab them!" The gamblers were shocked and desperately tried to escape by jumping out of windows and over walls. The gambling boss, Sha Jinggui from Chongming, and Gu Zhengquan from Pudong, as well as gamblers Xu Futao, Zhu Amao, Xu Fugun, Xi Sanmao, Zhang Musheng, Zhang Quange, Zhang Falang from Chongming, Wang Erlang, Wang Xiaojiang, and a total of eleven gamblers and drug offenders were arrested on the spot. A gambling cylinder, several dice, three decks of playing cards, four sets of mahjong tiles, a set of pai gow tiles, three opium pipes and red pill pipes, twenty-two dollars in opium gambling money, thirty-six cents in small coins, and chips were seized. They were all taken back to the team. Under interrogation, all the suspects confessed to gambling, smoking opium, and taking red pills. Captain Lu believed that the case involved gambling, skimming, and operating an opium den, which was illegal. He ordered that the eleven suspects and the gambling and drug paraphernalia be sent to the Third Section for legal action.

International Sleeping Car Changed to Through Train

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus received a telegraphed instruction from the Ministry of Railways stating that the Beijing-Shanghai Railway had inquired about the international sleeping car company's sleeping cars, which were restricted by contract from being attached to through trains jointly operated by Shanghai and Pingpu. The Ministry had stipulated that these sleeping cars should be temporarily attached to passenger trains 1 and 2 of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. The Pingjin section would be connected to passenger trains 5 and 6 of the Beining Railway. Orders were issued to comply with these instructions last month. It is now found that passenger trains 1 and 2 of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway have been changed to direct trains to Pingpu. All sleeping cars of the aforementioned international sleeping car company should be attached to passenger trains 1 and 2 of the Tianjin-Pukou through trains and should no longer be connected by passenger trains 5 and 6 of the Beining Railway. You are to inform the Bureau. Minister Gu Mengyu, Seal of Xiaolian. The Bureau has forwarded the instructions to the Transportation Department for compliance.

Seafarer Examination Moved to Shanghai

The Ministry of Transportation previously held a seafarer examination in Beijing in October. The China Marine Engineers' Association petitioned the Ministry, stating that it was inconvenient for seafarers to travel to Beijing for the examination due to wartime conditions. They requested that the examination be moved to Shanghai. The Ministry replied that the request was well-founded and approved it for consideration. The Ministry's Order No. 2395 and member Chuan Abao of the Association stated that the examination would be held in Shanghai on January 24, 1934. The examination location has been changed accordingly.

(1 item) Medical Affairs Compilation Issue No. 18 is approved to be published in advance at the time of the General Assembly. All reports on association affairs and finances for the past two years should be compiled quickly for printing. The Documentary Committee is requested to compile the report on association affairs, and the Economic Committee is requested to compile the financial report. (1 item) Should the proposals and rules of procedure for this General Assembly be revised? (Resolution) Xia Shenchu and Zhu Qiluo are requested to revise them. (1 item) Request to stipulate the procedures for admitting unjoined local doctors to the General Assembly. (Resolution) Local doctors from non-member organizations will be responsible for their own food and accommodation. (1 item) Request to stipulate the procedures for attending and observing the General Assembly. (Resolution) Members of each member organization, excluding the attending delegates, will serve as observers. New medical associations established throughout the country and organizations organized by formal doctors, even if they have not joined this association, will also be observers. Formal doctors from areas where such organizations do not exist who wish to attend the meeting will be auditors. (1 item) Stipulate the travel expenses for each executive and supervisory committee member to Beijing. (Resolution) The travel expenses for each executive and supervisory committee member will be fully borne by the Association, following the precedent of the previous session. (1 item) Should the General Assembly announcement be published in areas outside of Shanghai? (Resolution) Add Tianjin, Guangzhou, and Hankou. (1 item) Request to organize a committee to plan a national medical affairs outline and to appoint specialized committee members. (Resolution) Xu Naili, Xia Shenchu, Pang Jingzhou, Wang Qizhang, Cai Yumen, and Zhu Qiluo are appointed as specialized committee members. (1 item) The Shanghai Xinyi Pharmaceutical Factory intends to host a banquet for the delegates of the Third General Assembly. Please specify the date of the banquet first. (Resolution) To be decided when scheduling the General Assembly agenda.

Zhu Ziqiao and Others Visit the Mental Hospital

Gu Wenjun from Chuansha, based on his family's seven-generation tradition of specializing in the treatment of madness, combined with decades of clinical experience, came forward to serve the world and founded the Shanghai Mental Hospital in Ren'an Lane, Guling Road. Since its opening, it has achieved remarkable results. Yesterday afternoon, Zhu Ziqiao, Yan Mengfan, Shao Daren, and others visited the hospital together. Zhu said that patients with mental illness should be treated with tranquility. The hospital site should be in a remote location. It is a pity that financial problems are difficult to solve and it is not easy to set up. Today, the facilities of your hospital are quite complete, and the location is quiet in the midst of the bustling city. Director Gu, in his twilight years, is able to work tirelessly and is enthusiastic about charity, which is very commendable. Gu politely declined to comment. Zhu and others said that patients with mental illness are the most miserable people with illnesses and that treatment is extremely difficult, and they praised the hospital repeatedly. They then took their leave and departed.

Haijingbo Circus to Leave Shanghai in a Week

The Haijingbo Circus, currently performing in Shanghai, is scheduled to set sail for India in just one week. Counting back, the troupe has already been in Shanghai for seven weeks. During this time, thousands of spectators have flocked to see the show daily, making it a grand spectacle. It's no easy task to transport such a large circus all the way from Europe to the East, but Haijingbo resolutely undertook it, believing that the Far East tour would be highly profitable. Today, business is indeed very good. With the weather turning colder, the troupe uses large stoves to burn in the tents before each performance, making the air inside exceptionally warm. Recently, the circus clowns have added new tricks to entertain the audience, and Auden's mixed animal show has added two new and amazing performances, which are quite spectacular. Its famous zoo attracts many visitors, open daily from 10:00 AM to 6:00 PM. Tickets are priced at five jiao for adults and two jiao for children. Animal feeding takes place every day at 11:00 AM, except on Mondays.

Pudong: Electrical Company Expands Power Supply; Extends Lines to Zhoupu Town in Nanhui County; Supplies Daming Electrical Company for Resale

The Pudong Electric Company extended its lines to Beicai Town and Zhangjiangzha Town in Nanhui County in April of this year to supply electricity to Huibei Electric Company for distribution to households. It has been half a year since then, and the results have been remarkable. In rural towns and villages, modern facilities of all kinds are lacking, but electricity is the first to take root. Not only is the supply plentiful and the pressure sufficient, but the lines crisscross the area, providing electricity day and night, which is particularly noteworthy. Therefore, since Huibei Electric Company started receiving electricity, it has been warmly welcomed by local people, resulting in a surge in users and a thriving business. Moreover, its engineering operations and management are coordinated and cooperate with Pudong Electric Company, so its operations are well-managed and can serve as a model for rural power plants. Zhoupu Town, a prosperous commercial center in the vicinity, is second to none among the towns in Nanhui County. The existing Daming Electric Company has a generator that is too small to meet the demand, and it uses direct current, which cannot transmit voltage over long distances. Seeing the success of Huibei Electric Company in purchasing and reselling electricity, it has also voluntarily stopped generating electricity and requested Pudong Electric Company to supply it. After repeated consultations, a draft contract of 19 articles has been agreed upon, which has been submitted by Pudong Electric Company to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities and forwarded to the Municipal Government, which has instructed its approval. A formal signing will take place in the next few days. Pudong Electric Company will initially be responsible for supplying a maximum demand of 200 kilowatts, and then gradually increase it year by year to meet the needs of expansion. After the contract is signed, Pudong Electric Company will lay high-voltage lines eastward from Sanlin Town along the Shangnan Long-Distance Bus Road directly to Zhoupu Town, first installing two 60-kilowatt transformers. It is estimated that the project can be completed and the electricity supplied within two months.

Jiang Xiaojian Invents Ding-Yi Style Coal-Saving Stove

Artist Jiang Xiaojian has recently established the Meifeng Bronze Foundry on Hongqiao Road. In addition to sculpting and casting bronze statues, he also uses boiler machinery to produce various carved metal artworks during his off-hours. In view of the unsightly designs and coal-consuming nature of the stoves sold on the market, he has independently researched and manufactured a new type of stove. Its exterior is shaped like the bronze tripods and vessels of the Xia, Shang, and Zhou dynasties, and it is equipped with a new type of ventilated firebrick inside, so it consumes very little coal, even less than the imported Junkers stoves. This stove will soon be available in large quantities and is said to be sold through the Home Industry Cooperative, National Goods Company, and department stores.

News of the Soon-to-Open Grand Shanghai Theater

The magnificent architecture and luxurious equipment of the Grand Shanghai Theater have been briefly described in previous reports. It is now known that the theater has not only put great effort into its construction and equipment, but also makes every effort to select films and manage them strictly. The theater has signed exclusive screening contracts with the American Fox and RKO film companies, and the blockbusters of 1934 will all be screened at the theater. The opening film is Fox's super special production, "Lily of the Alley" starring Lilian Harvey, followed by "The World Changes" starring Paul Muni, and "Little Miss Marker" starring Shirley Temple. It is also heard that the ticket sales and ushering staff of the theater are well-trained and will absolutely not allow any slow or rude service. The ticket prices will be charged according to the market exchange rate for small coins, and the grease money that Shanghai residents have long been disgusted with will not be tolerated in the theater. There are four Chinese and four Western female ushers upstairs to treat guests equally, without any discrimination. The program notes are written by experts and are concise and readable, perfectly matching the plot. The vendors in the theater are neatly dressed and sell at fair prices. Other aspects are also being strengthened in an effort to give the people of Shanghai a refreshing experience.

Fire in Pudong

At around 2:11 PM yesterday, a fire broke out at the Zhenhua Liji Textile Factory, No. 4 Lan Road, Yangshupu, where the lower level is a cotton ginning room. Sparks from the machinery flew into the cotton, causing a sudden fire. Smoke filled the air, and flames soared. The male and female workers in the workshop swarmed out in a very chaotic manner. The fire brigade rushed to the scene to put out the fire, which was extinguished after more than an hour. Because the factory foundation is built of cement, it is not easy to catch fire. Only the cotton was burned and water damaged, with a loss of about 400 taels. It is said to be covered by fire insurance.

At around 6:40 PM last night, a fire broke out in an unnumbered bungalow opposite the China General Omnibus Company at the junction of Kangnao Road and the French Concession in West Shanghai, burning down three houses. The fire brigade rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire.

Taxpayers' Association Appeals for Slum Dwellers; Sends Letter to the Public Works Department for Sympathy

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association sent a letter to Zhong Siyun, Director-General of the Public Works Department of the Shanghai International Settlement, yesterday, stating that the Jianghuai Association in Shanghai had received a letter from its members Xu Xijin, Gu Baoan, Xu Xizhong, and 51 others, stating that the shacks inhabited by the poor were located in a piece of wasteland east of Qiqihar Road, Yangshupu, which was originally a swamp. The landlord told the poor that if they filled in the land, they could build shacks and live there for 10 or 8 years without any fixed term. The poor people, having no money, believed his words and first filled in a small portion of the swamp, building four or five huts. After the Sino-Japanese War, more and more poor people came, so they filled in a section of the swamp, building one shack at a time. To date, it has been four years, and the swamp has been completely filled in, and the shacks are fully occupied. There are still traces of the swamp that can be used as evidence. There are more than 30 households on the two streets. The landlord on the west side is Xu Weiren, who collects 30 yuan in rent each year, and the one on the east side is Xu Xiaofu, who collects 50 yuan each year, with the rent due on the fifth month of each year, and no arrears are allowed. On the fifth day of the fifth month of this year, the poor people paid the rent in full. The land rent is collected by Shen Xisheng every year. Unexpectedly, in June of this year, the Health Bureau, due to the disorderly shacks and unsanitary conditions, specifically notified the poor people to rebuild them into three rows for the sake of hygiene. The poor people had no choice but to rebuild them according to the regulations, which really left them destitute. During the rebuilding process, which took about two weeks to complete, the landlord was not seen to interfere. Unexpectedly, after only a month of living there, the landlord had ill intentions. He went back on his word, bullied the poor and favored the rich, and subleased the land to the Hongda Rubber Factory to build a factory, forcing the poor to relocate immediately. Although they are shacks, each one costs about 30 yuan to build. The poor people borrowed from all sides with great difficulty, and now they want to demolish them. In the cold winter, they have no home to return to, and it is difficult to find shelter in the open. The lives of more than 100 people, old and young, will surely freeze to death on the road and die in the ditches. This is truly unbearable to hear and see. Alas, the landlord uses such oppressive means, in addition to mobilizing the police and Bao Tiao to intimidate them, and has asked lawyer Xu Zaiyi to issue a notice, limiting them to demolishing everything within a week, and there is no time to lose. If this is true, the poor people have no way to go to heaven and no door to enter the earth.

The letter continues, "The poor people were promised by Xu Weiren and others that they could fill in the pond land with their labor and live there for a long time, and they have paid the rent every year without any shortage. This is a legitimate lease relationship with proper procedures and legal behavior. It should not be described as unauthorized construction. Even if the land is taken back for use, the residents should be given sufficient preparation time and should not be forced to do so immediately, let alone subleased to a third party instead of being taken back for self-use. Moreover, in June of this year, the residents were ordered by the Health Bureau to rebuild the two rows into three rows, avoiding economic losses, and they have already suffered greatly. Their vitality has not yet recovered, and now, in the severe cold, they are suddenly ordered to demolish the houses and relocate within a week, which will inevitably expose more than 100 people to the elements and endanger their lives. This is not only unfair in terms of reason and logic, but also not what the municipal authorities would want to see. Therefore, we are sending a copy of lawyer Xu's notice and writing to your council, requesting that the Bureau of Public Works and the municipal authorities take public opinion into consideration and handle the matter with caution, or postpone it until the spring of next year, when the weather is warmer, and let our association find an address for them to relocate to, in order to relieve the poor and avoid disputes. We hope you will investigate and handle the matter accordingly."

After reviewing the letter, the association stated that the case is a dispute between the landlord and the tenants. According to the law and the previous correspondence between the Bureau and the Council on this matter, it is certain that the police will not be sent to enforce the landlord's order. This is what the Association firmly believes. However, as it is now severe winter, and these poor slum dwellers have no home and are exposed to the elements, for the sake of public order and humanity, the municipal authorities can certainly provide considerable assistance from a political standpoint. Accordingly, the Council is requested to examine the matter and, within the scope of the law, show deep sympathy for the slum dwellers.

Inspection Report of the Central Bank, No. 179

The 179th inspection report on the issuance reserves of the Central Bank states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserves for the issuance of convertible banknotes of the Bank. The 179th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the Bank on November 20, 1933. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 68,917,830 silver dollars, including 63,196,231 silver dollar notes and 5,721,599 fractional currency notes. Total amount of convertible banknote reserves: 68,917,830 silver dollars, including 56,359,830 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve includes 52,700,951 silver dollars stored in the Bank's issuance vault, 1,872,680 silver dollars stored in the branches in various ports, and 1,777,199 silver dollars deposited with correspondent banks. Guarantee reserves equivalent to 12,558,000 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of Customs Gold Unit convertible banknotes issued: 416,715.40 yuan. Total amount of Customs Gold Unit convertible banknote reserves: 416,715.40 yuan. This reserve includes 6,995.39 taels of standard gold, valued at 5957 Customs Gold Units, equivalent to 416,715.40 yuan. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted." November 21, 1933. Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank: Li Fuxun. Supervisors: Xie Mingdong, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kangqin, Xu Jilao.

Tao Erbao Sentenced to Life Imprisonment for Premeditated Murder

Tao Erbao of Wusong was a vagrant, so his younger sister, Tao Xiaomei, who was of marriageable age, had not yet found a husband. As a result, she was seduced and became romantically involved, and was sold as a concubine to Li Xigen, the owner of the Hongsheng Paper Store in Caojiadu. When Tao Erbao returned home and learned of the situation, he felt that since his sister had become a concubine, he, as the elder brother, had not received any bride price, so he went to borrow 500 yuan. As a result, he was given 30 yuan, which he was not satisfied with, and left. On the evening of October 2, at 8:00 PM, thugs came to the store and shot Li Xigen to death. After the wife of the deceased, Li Zhao, reported to the Detective Team, Tao Erbao was arrested. He was transferred to the Local Court by the Public Security Bureau, and the prosecutor filed a public prosecution against him for premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Code. After a hearing and debate, Judge Guan opened the court yesterday afternoon and sentenced Tao Erbao to life imprisonment for premeditated murder, with deprivation of civil rights for life. The judge said that according to the law, the crime was punishable by death, but the sentence was reduced to life imprisonment. Tao Erbao was not satisfied, and the judge told him that he could appeal according to the law. He was then ordered to be taken back into custody.

Chen Qinxi Sentenced to Life Imprisonment for Aiding and Abetting Murder

Yan Zhang (aka Li Azhang), 21 years old, from Ningbo, lived at No. 24 Taopeng Road. Previously, he had a deep grudge against a fellow townsman named Ahua over the issue of a handgun. As a result, at around 9:00 PM on August 22, Ahua, together with Xiang Xiasheng, who had already been sentenced to imprisonment, and Chen Xi, Zhang Quan, Xiaobiao, and others who were at large, lured Azhang to a remote and dark place near Guiyang Road and Chegong Road under the pretext of taking a stroll to cool off. Ahua then took out a pistol and shot Azhang. Azhang was hit in a vital part of his body, fell to the ground, and called for help. Zhang Quan and Chen Xi then took off his pants, pushed him into a small ditch, and hoped that he would die quickly. Afterwards, the Chinese and Western detectives from the police station in charge of the area found him and arranged for him to be sent to the Sacred Heart Hospital, where he died of his injuries. On the 5th of this month, Su Changsheng, the Chinese detective chief of the Yulin Road Police Station, and Detective Xie Wanfang arrested Chen Xi (aka Chen Qinxi) on Yuezhou Road and sent him to the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, requested that the defendant be severely punished because of his cruel methods. The court issued an order to await sentencing. As reported in this newspaper, yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Xiefen presided over the Third Criminal Court and sentenced Chen Qinxi to life imprisonment for the crime of aiding and abetting murder.

Liu Heshang Falls to His Death

Liu Heshang, a local resident, 26 years old, was a plasterer. At around 4:00 PM yesterday, Liu was working at the Chinese Securities Exchange on Sanma Road when he accidentally fell from the upper floor, seriously injuring his head. He was barely breathing. The foreman of the construction company immediately reported the incident to the police station, and the police were ordered to arrive. Suicide at the Gongping Inn

A traveler who identified himself as Yao Liancheng, a local resident, 30 years old, engaged in the printing business, arrived at the Gongping Inn at the entrance of Baoyu Lane, Edward Road in the French Concession the day before yesterday (the 19th). Due to economic difficulties, he was at his wit's end and had the idea of ending his life. Yesterday afternoon, he committed suicide by swallowing a large amount of Sheng Sheng Yan (a brand of rat poison). The porter noticed and immediately hired a streetcar to send him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died at around 6:00 PM in the evening. Afterwards, Bao Tiao Wang Licheng went to investigate and sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall to await examination.

Two Died Unnaturally

(1) Qian Deren, a 20-year-old worker from Taixing at the Huayang Textile Factory behind the Sanyoutang on Lujiabang in Nanshi, was working in the dyeing and finishing department at 12:00 PM yesterday when, due to carelessness, his sleeve was caught by the silk-finishing wheel belt, and he was crushed into it, resulting in a bloody mess. His colleagues saw this and immediately stopped the machine to rescue him, but he had already died. The factory accountant then reported the situation to the Second District Police Station, which sent police to the scene for investigation. They then ordered Bao Gu Xueyuan to report the incident to the Local Court for examination. Inspector Kong and forensic doctor Zhang Huazhong were dispatched to the scene and confirmed that the death was caused by being crushed. They ordered the factory to collect the body and await verification. (2) Yesterday, an elderly man of about 60 years of age fell off the bridge at Guojia Stone Bridge in Donggou, Pudong. He hit his head on the bridge stone, causing a head injury, and fell into the river and drowned. By the time the body was recovered, it was impossible to save him. The passers-by reported the incident to the Third Section of the Fifth District, which ordered Xu Jinsheng, the Bao of the Twelfth Tu of the Twenty-second Bao, to report the incident to the Local Court for examination. Inspector Kong and others were dispatched to the scene and confirmed that the death was caused by a fall and drowning. They ordered the Bao to investigate and summon the family members to collect the body.

Zhang Hanliang Attempts Suicide After Losing His Job

On the evening of the day before yesterday, a young man boarded a municipal ferry at the Dongmen Road Pier and jumped into the Huangpu River to commit suicide. Fortunately, the old captain noticed and immediately stopped the engine and tried to rescue him. When the ship arrived in Pudong, he was sent to the Third District. According to his confession, his name was Zhang Hanliang, 28 years old, from Wuxing, Zhejiang, and he lived at No. 12 Guanyin Bridge, Shaowu Town, North Gate, Huzhou. He was previously a manager at the Qichang Yong Silk Factory in Zhabei. He was dismissed seven or eight months ago and formed a partnership with a friend to rent a house at No. 12 Gonghe Road. Recently, his friend returned to Huzhou, so he gave up the house a few days ago. He had been staying in Room 55 of the Southeast Hotel for two days. Because he had run out of money, and thinking that he had been unemployed for a long time and had no hope for the future, he had the idea of ending his life. He still had a mother at home, and he was not yet married. He had worked in Shanghai for 13 years, but because he loved to gamble, he had no savings. Once he lost his job, he had no face to return home. This was the reason for his suicide. The District Chief, feeling that his situation was very pitiful, ordered him to be sent to the Headquarters for assistance.

Verdict on Counterfeit Three Flower Cold Cream Trademark

The Three Flower Cold Cream produced by the American company Hedner has been sold in China for more than ten years. The trademark was first used in China in 1918 and was verified by the Trademark Bureau. The Trademark Bureau issued Reassessment Document No. 21 on May 9 of this year. In July of last year, the Tianshu Industrial Company on Wuzhou Road in this city manufactured and sold Three Hua Cream, imitating the trademark of the cold cream. The structure of the entire pattern on the box, the colors used, the arrangement method, and the layout of the patterns were all very similar. In October of last year, Garnay, the representative of Hedner in Shanghai, discovered this and reported it to the Jiaxing Road Police Station, which seized many counterfeit trademark goods and filed a lawsuit. The case was heard by the First Special District Court and the debate ended last month. The verdict was announced on the first day of this month. The main text of the verdict stated that Zhu Zhonghe (the manager of the company) intended to deceive others by counterfeiting the trademark and was sentenced to two months of imprisonment, suspended for two years. All 744 bottles of Three Hua Cream, 908 small empty paper boxes, 55 trademark papers, and 48 hard papers were confiscated. The reasons for the verdict are too long to be recorded in full.

Chen Zhegao Celebrates His Fiftieth Birthday

Chen Zhegao of Wumen has lived in Shanghai for more than ten years and has friends all over the world. He is generous and righteous, helping the weak and supporting the poor, and has the style of an ancient knight. Yesterday, he celebrated his fiftieth birthday, and his friends celebrated his birthday with a banquet at the Hushe Restaurant on Beijing Road. Celebrities and dignitaries from all walks of life came one after another, including Huang Jinrong, Wang Yiting, and Yuan Ludeng. The art and calligraphy circles were the most prominent, and the gifts they presented were mostly paintings and calligraphy, which were displayed in a room, resembling a grand art and calligraphy exhibition. The staff, including Zhu Jingfang, Chen Xianglin, Xu Jinchun, Qiu Zijia, Feng Mengyun, and others, were all his students. Female stars Xuan Jinglin, Xu Qinfang, and Fan Xuepeng, as well as male opera amateurs Rong Boming, Shen Yizhen, Gong Zhaoxiong, Xie Wenyuan, and Zhan Xiaoshan, performed Peking opera at the hall. The entire orchestra of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau played music all day long. In the afternoon, Chen Jun took a family photo in the auditorium and a group photo with all his students on the roof. The party did not end until midnight.

Publication of Improved Kunqu Opera Scripts

The improved Kunqu opera scripts were compiled by Xu Zhongheng. The lyrics are accurate and annotated with gongche scores. The dialogue for each character is arranged in separate lines, making it very eye-catching. Each opera is sold as a single volume, making it very convenient to carry. The book also includes inscriptions by Wang Xiaolai, Mu Ouchu, Yu Zhenfei, Xu Lingyun, Xu Ziquan, Jiang Yusheng, and Gao Hansheng, as well as calligraphy by Kunqu opera stars Zhu Fuming and Shi Fuzhen, which adds to its appeal. The published works include "Good Time to Press for an Answer", "Chunxiang Creates a Disturbance in the School", "Assassinating Hu", "Wandering in the Garden and Startled by a Dream", "Xu Ge Listens to the Bell", "Sweeping Flowers Thrice Drunk", "Thinking of Mortality", "Dressing Up and Kneeling by the Pond", "Zhaojun Marries the Barbarians", and "Qin Challenges". They are published by Xiaoxing Bookstore on Qipan Street and cost 0.10 yuan each. They are currently on sale at a special discount of 20% off.
