The Astuteness of a Tobacco and Paper Shop Apprentice: Robbery and Recovery of Stolen Goods

Ge Xiunian, an 18-year-old apprentice from Suzhou at Hao Xiangwei Tobacco and Paper Shop, located at No. 85 Pushi Road in the French Concession, was instructed by his employer to take four hundred and fifty silver dollars in cash to the Hengfengtai Tobacco and Paper Exchange in Zhengjia Wood Bridge to exchange for copper coins on the morning of the 20th at around 9:00 AM. As Ge was passing by the Xiaocaichang (small vegetable market) near the Eight Immortals Bridge, two robbers wearing yellow and blue cloth short shirts and trousers and speaking in the local dialect suddenly rushed up and blocked his way. One robber grabbed Ge, while the other seized a package of banknotes from Ge's side and fled. Fortunately, Ge was astute, recognized the robber who snatched the money, and gave chase, shouting loudly to catch the thief. Hearing the cries, patrol officers arrived and helped to apprehend the robber. The original stolen goods were found on his person. He was taken to the police station where, under interrogation by the police chief, he confessed his name as Xue Renzhong, 28 years old, from Pudong, unemployed, and residing in a hostel. He admitted to conspiring with an accomplice at large to commit robbery. The police chief, upon hearing the confession, ordered his detention. Yesterday afternoon, he was sent to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court where he was interrogated by Judge Li Changnian. Yuan Jiahong, a lawyer from the police station, presented the case, stating that the defendant was arrested for robbery. The police are still investigating and need to apprehend the accomplice. He requested a postponement of the trial. He then presented the recovered stolen money as evidence. Following this, the victim described the circumstances of the robbery. The court, upon reviewing the evidence, briefly questioned the defendant and ordered him to be remanded in custody pending a rescheduled trial.

News from Various Native Place Associations

The Guangdong Native Place Association in Shanghai held its ninth board meeting yesterday. Directors Chen Fengyuan, Chen Qifen, Weng Ziguang, Pan Zhiquan, Wen Hongen, Wu Chengyu, Tang Haian, Wu Tiecheng (representing Li Dachao) attended. Supervisors Wu Jishun, Physician Wu Jiangleng also attended. Tang Haian presided and Lu Yuquan recorded the minutes. Matters reported included: (1) Chairman Tang reported on the payment for the purchase of the association's building. The full price of the building's land, fifty-three thousand taels of silver, had been paid. The income from donations, after deducting the association's and hospital's routine expenses, repaying old debts of the hospital, and paying for the building, was still short by eight thousand silver dollars. These funds had been advanced by individuals. As this concerned the public good of our hometown, they dared not calculate interest. If the association's finances were to become difficult, they would not dare to request repayment. However, the hospital and the association still required fifty thousand dollars for future purchases. It seemed necessary to continue fundraising to achieve complete success. The property deed had been handed over to the association, and a proposal was made to elect custodians to ensure due solemnity. It was resolved that efforts should be made to raise donations to repay the eight thousand dollars as soon as possible. The method of fundraising would be discussed after moving to the new location. The deed would be kept by Director Tang to ensure its solemn custody. Matters discussed included: (1) Director Wu Tiecheng proposed setting a date and formalities for the opening of the new location and selecting preparatory staff in advance to facilitate the event. It was resolved to appoint directors Chen Fengyuan, Xi Guansheng, Li Dachao, Chen Qifen, Weng Ziguang, Yang Meinan, and Pan Zhiquan as preparatory staff, convened by Li Dachao. The preparatory committee would plan all the opening procedures and submit them to the board of directors for approval. Temporary motions: (2) Supervisor Wu Jishun proposed purchasing medical equipment for the hospital, which had arrived from Germany, and requested the allocation of three thousand dollars for payment. He also proposed dissolving the executive committee of the Guangdong People's Hospital to centralize authority. It was resolved that the previous resolution to allocate three thousand dollars would be implemented after the goods arrived from Germany and a bill was submitted for approval. Regarding the dissolution of the executive committee, reasons should be presented to the association, and the matter would be discussed at the next meeting. (3) Physician Wu Jiangleng reported on his investigation into the dispute between physicians Wu Jingyao and Chen Daming. Both sides realized their errors, which seemed to be misunderstandings. It was resolved to publicly recommend that Director Chen Fengyuan and Physician Wu Jiangleng revisit both parties to convey the association's intention to promote harmony and provide sincere explanations.

The Fenghua Native Place Association in Shanghai held its fifth election convention at the Ningbo Native Place Association yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM. Over one thousand three hundred people attended. Wu Zhihao, Chen Zhonggao, Yu Hualong, Wang Shijia, and Wang Jitao were publicly elected as the presidium, with Chen Siyu as the master of ceremonies. The order of proceedings was as follows: (1) Musical performance. (2) Formal ceremonies. (3) The chairman delivered an opening speech, details omitted. (4) Director Chen Zhonggao reported on the association's affairs, which had handled over a thousand cases of disaster relief, dispute resolution, and recovery of lost women and children. The secretary Wu Chongchen reported on the recruitment of points. The Zhengting team had the highest number of points and should be awarded a gold cup. Other teams that met the reward regulations were given silver cups, silver shields, gold district awards, and certificates. (5) Yu Hualong proposed publicly electing ten ballot counters, including Ma Donghai. Ballots were counted on the spot, overseen by the chairman. (6) Guest speakers Yu Sicai and Chen Liangwang gave speeches, details omitted. (7) Refreshments and photography. (8) Results were announced. The first round of elections resulted in sixty nominees: Wu Zhihao with 1306 votes, Wang Zhengting with 1253 votes, Zhuang Jieshi with 1054 votes, Chen Zhonggao with 1051 votes, and Jin Hualong with 1042 votes. Details of the remaining vote counts were not recorded.

New Invention: Pigment Mercury Disinfectant: While many disinfectants have appeared on the market recently, truly perfect medications are still rare. Recently, Li Chao of the Capital Nanjing Commercial Cooperative Society's laboratory has, through diligent study and extensive experimentation, invented the pigment mercury disinfectant. The product's advantage is that it does not burn the skin and has no irritating properties. It has a certificate of analysis from the Health Testing Laboratory, so it is often used as a disinfectant for surgical procedures. For conditions such as pneumonia, erysipelas, scarlet fever, diphtheria, syphilis, etc., a solution of one part per thousand is used for washing and gargling. It can also prevent infectious diseases. For knife wounds, broken skin, and scrofula, it can be used as a topical application, capable of disinfecting, removing decay, and closing wounds. The majority of its raw materials are domestically produced. It is reported that major hospitals and physicians both locally and abroad are happy to adopt it, so sales are very active. Major pharmacies selling pigment mercury are competing to order goods.

New Use for Hot Water Bottles: Any high-temperature water bottle can be used to cook porridge and stew soup. Therefore, economical families often adopt this method, as it requires no fuel cost. According to a certain gentleman, his family has three Tiantan brand domestic water bottles. One is used to cook porridge for his young daughter's breakfast, one is used to cook lotus seed soup for his and his wife's occasional snack, and another is used to cook white fungus for his elderly mother's nourishment. Assuming the cost of each type of fuel is just over three cents, one month would be three dollars, so thirty-six dollars can be saved annually.

The store operates on the principle of production and sales cooperation, implementing the goal of selling high-quality goods at low prices. The low prices of various factories' silk and satin are unprecedented. At the time of the grand opening, the dyeing workshops were closed, so various patterned silk and satin fabrics could not be fully supplied. Now that the dyeing workshops have resumed work, to thank everyone, the store officially opened yesterday and presented silk and satin clothing materials as gifts. It is said that business was very prosperous throughout the day yesterday.

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong coast was cloudy with strong winds from the northwest to north. The middle and upper reaches of the Yangtze River and the coast here were cloudy with fog or rain, and mild cyclones due to a low pressure system moving northeast-east or east. The coastal area south of Ma'an Island had mild northeasterly to southeasterly winds. Also, at 3:00 PM yesterday, the local temperature in the previous 24 hours was a high of 74.3 degrees and a low of 44.6 degrees. The Ministry of Education of the Central Government is Devising Methods to Supervise the Independence of Educational Funding in Various Provinces and Cities; It Dispatched Personnel Yesterday to Negotiate with the Beijing Municipal Government

(Nanjing, 21st) To ensure the stability of education, the Ministry of Education is devising methods to supervise the independence of educational funding in various provinces and cities. On the 21st, it dispatched Inspector and Secretary-General Zhong Daozan to the Municipal Government to hold preliminary discussions with Director Wang of the Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau regarding the procedures for independent educational funding in Beijing. As the Ministry of Education ordered the establishment of practical vocational education methods in Beijing, the Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau is currently drafting plans and will submit them to the Ministry of Education within a week.

The Ministry of Education Issues a Circular to Various Departments and Bureaus, Forwarding Orders Regarding Military Training Procedures for Senior Vocational Schools

(Nanjing, 21st) The Ministry of Education issued a circular to various departments and bureaus, forwarding orders to senior vocational schools regarding military training procedures. For students who are admitted after graduating from junior high school, the military training hours will be changed to two hours per week in the first and second academic years, from the originally scheduled three hours. For those who are admitted after graduating from elementary school, the military training hours will be changed to two hours per week in the fourth and fifth academic years.

Ministry of Education Inspector Guo Youshou Returns to Beijing, Stating that Education in Qingdao, Shandong Province, is Stable

(Nanjing, 21st) Ministry of Education Inspector Guo Youshou concluded his inspection of education in Qingdao, Shandong Province, and visited Chairman Han in Jinan to discuss the inspection process. He returned to the Ministry of Education on the 21st. He stated that education in Qingdao, Shandong Province, is stable, and his overall impression of the inspection was very positive.

The Counties and County Bureau Chiefs of Jiangsu Province Recognized for Their Meritorious Service in Collecting and Transferring Educational Funding Over the Past Five Years

Since the independence of educational funding in Jiangsu Province, the counties have been required to transfer the educational funding collected from the busy tax revenue to the organizations responsible for managing educational funding. The province has established methods for assessing county magistrates and finance bureau chiefs regarding the collection and transfer of special educational funds. If a county magistrate or finance bureau chief has fully transferred the special educational funds that should be collected in the county without any arrears for more than a year, they may receive commendation from the provincial departments and bureaus. Over the years from 1928 to the present, there have been many county magistrates or finance bureau chiefs who have been commended and rewarded by the provincial departments and bureaus for their meritorious service in collecting educational funding. The following is a summary:

(1) In 1928, Zhou Hao, magistrate of Jiangning County; Liu Xiuyue, magistrate of Liuhe County; Wu Xiangrong, magistrate of Kunshan County; Wu Bangzhen, magistrate of Wujiang County; Ding Zuozhe, magistrate of Taixing County; Wu Bogeng, magistrate of Jiading County; Zheng Liduo, magistrate of Wujin County.

(2) In 1930, Zhang Lixun, finance bureau chief of Danyang; Bei Jietai, finance bureau chief of Baoshan; Chen Liangdong, finance bureau chief of Luxi.

(3) In 1931, Wang Shenggao, finance bureau chief of Huai'an.

(4) In 1932, Chen Zujun, finance bureau chief of Qingpu (hereinafter "finance" is omitted); Li Shiyi, bureau chief of Fengxian; Hu Baojing, bureau chief of Kunshan; Wang Huazhao, bureau chief of Shanghai; Wang Shenggao, bureau chief of Changshu (Wang received two major awards); Wang Zhaojia, bureau chief of Zhenjiang.

(5) Most recently in 1933, Cheng Yuyi, magistrate of Xinghua County, and Li Leng, magistrate of Chuansha County, have requested awards.

For the county magistrates and bureau chiefs listed above who have made meritorious contributions to the collection and transfer of educational funding, their request for awards will be submitted to the provincial government for discussion and approval, and they will be recorded with a major merit once.

The Shanghai University Student Federation, believing that the Minbian (Fujian Incident) was manipulated and directed by Chen Mingshu alone, sent a cable yesterday condemning him, stating: Chen Zhenru of Fuzhou, Your Excellency, Reports state that you have colluded with elements of the so-called Third Party, established your own banner, and implemented a rebellion. Those near and far are shocked and dismayed. The country is facing the adversity of foreign aggression and domestic troubles, and the people are trapped in dire suffering. Even with a united effort to save the situation, we fear it may be insufficient. Yet you, sir, are willing to act perversely, further disrupting the life of the country with turmoil. We do not know what your intentions are. The national crisis is so severe, the only way is to unite with common hatred of the enemy and defend against insults. Otherwise, speaking of resisting Japan and saving the country is simply using ulterior motives and is ultimately betraying the party and the country. Wisdom, foolishness, virtue, and wickedness - it is for you to choose. Shanghai University Student Federation, bowing in respect. (Ma)

The End of the Wuben School Disturbance 丨Joint Statement by the Old and New Principals丨

Regarding the recent student disturbance at the Municipal Wuben Girls' High School due to opposition to the Director of Studies, various newspapers have carried different accounts. Some involve the former principal, Wang Xiaoying, and the China Girls' High School, while others involve other teachers and staff who resigned voluntarily. As a result, the truth is unclear and misunderstandings abound. The new and former principals (husband and wife), as well as several teachers and staff who resigned voluntarily, were invited by the new principal to a dinner at the Atlantic Western Restaurant yesterday. They each recounted the course of the school disturbance, clarifying the truth and dispelling misunderstandings. They jointly issued the following statement: It has been found that the school disturbance at Wuben occurred one week after the new principal took office, clearly unrelated to the principal's appointment. Subsequently, the following issues led to misunderstandings in various quarters. In order to clarify the truth for those who care about the school, explanations are provided below, item by item:

(1) The Process of Establishing the Student Union: At the beginning of the school disturbance, there were suspicions that the student union was being used as a weapon. In fact, during the summer vacation, the school had already received instructions from the Special Municipal Party Department to organize a student union. At that time, the former principal had already decided to resign and was awaiting the Education Bureau to find a successor. Therefore, apart from maintaining regular classes, they were unwilling to hold other extracurricular activities. Later, the Municipal Party Department repeatedly urged them to establish it within two weeks. They had no choice but to instruct the Dean of Students to notify the students of the general idea of the instructions for their own decision, to show that they would no longer be responsible for guidance. Judging from this, the organization of the student union was merely a routine school matter and did not have any special mission.

(2) The Handover Process between the Old and New Principals: After the school disturbance began, there were rumors that the former principal was unwilling to hand over duties. In fact, on the day the new principal was announced, the former principal advised them to take over as soon as possible and arrive at the school to take office early, to avoid the school's spirit from dissipating. Therefore, the new principal was announced on the third day, and at 10:00 AM the next morning, the former principal personally went to the school to hand over duties with the heads of each department. As for the financial part, because the budget for the 893 months of this year must await the Education Bureau's budget decision before the final accounts can be prepared, submitted to the bureau for approval and reimbursement, and the temporary expenses approved by the Education Bureau in the past and the regular expenses for October have not yet been received, so there is still a part that cannot be transferred. The rest has been transferred clearly, and the facts are all there. The so-called unclear handover and inability to take over are all groundless rumors.

(3) Student Representatives Going to China Girls' High School for Meetings: Because the China Girls' High School is close to Wuben, some junior high school students in the first and second grades came to the school for tutoring. Those with ulterior motives deliberately spread rumors, referring to the tutoring students as representatives of the Wuben Student Union. In fact, the Wuben student representatives, except for one occasion when the new principal sent three students to plead with teacher Chen Guiru to withdraw their resignation, had been to China Girls' High School (including Fang Xiuzhi, who was suspended this time). All senior students and student union representatives have never been there once. The teachers and staff of China Girls' High School are confident that they still have a considerable understanding of education and will never allow the school to be a place of right and wrong, arbitrarily destroying education and destroying youth, and convicting themselves as sinners in the education world.

(4) The Truth about the Fuse of the School Disturbance: Among the teachers at Wuben, one teacher had occasional misunderstandings with one or two students during class and suspected that they were being instigated by a former department head. As a result, misunderstandings arose and there were complaints from time to time. The speaker had no intention, but the listener took it to heart, and the word spread, resulting in errors. In fact, these were all personal conflicts, and the scope of the words was not related to China Girls' High School. Those close to the new principal mistakenly believed that it had a lot to do with the school. When the new Director of Studies arrived at the school, the school disturbance broke out, and various parties were thus led to layers of misunderstandings. The school disturbance almost became irreparable due to various misunderstandings. Fortunately, the new and former principals were originally classmates and both took education as their standpoint and caring for Wuben as the premise, opened their hearts and spoke frankly, and had a joint conversation. Some teachers also attended the meeting and stated that their usual remarks were all personal matters and had nothing to do with the school. Unexpectedly, someone relayed the rumors from it, causing this misunderstanding. The new and former principals were very satisfied that the layers of misunderstandings were dispelled in one day. Although the opening of China Girls' High School was delayed, classes have resumed as usual. The principal of the school will report the process to the director, and there is no problem. A case has been clarified to the world and can be concluded from now on.

The United States Will Not Participate in the Next Olympic Games If Germany Excludes Jewish Athletes The United States Issues a Warning Letter to Germany

(Pittsburgh, 20th Reuters) The National Congress of the American Athletic Association today resolved to send a letter of admonition to Germany regarding the treatment of German Jews. The Congress passed a motion requesting the International Olympic Committee to notify Germany that if German Jewish athletes are not allowed to train and prepare to participate in the 1936 Olympic Games, the United States will not participate at that time.

The three winning teams in last night's women's basketball games were all from the Southeast Women's Physical Education Teachers' College, and all were one-sided. Ren Shujiao was like a swimming dragon, and it was truly a sight to behold. The details are described below:

Ms. Liu Wenhua Scores Three Consecutive Goals

Miss Mali Flies into a Rage

Report on the Start of the 5th China Youth Basketball League

The basketball league sponsored by the Shanghai YMCA has been held for four years. The number of participating teams has increased year by year. In the previous session, a total of 51 teams joined, divided into two groups, business and academic. As a result of the competition, the skills and experience of each team have increased a lot. In order to promote it, the association will continue to hold this session and has hired Yue Xiurong, Shu Hong, Zhou Jiaqi, and Peng Sanmei as members of this session's committee. At yesterday's meeting, the league regulations were agreed upon as follows:

Shanghai China YMCA Basketball League Regulations

1. Name: Shanghai China YMCA Basketball League (referred to as China Youth Basketball League)

2. Purpose: To seek more opportunities for each team to compete, so as to exchange skills, increase experience and interest.

3. Qualifications: Regardless of schools, organizations, institutions, or companies, anyone who is interested in this sport can form a team to participate (however, teams and members who have joined the China Sports Association or the West Youth Basketball Association are not allowed to participate).

4. Registration: From now until December 9th. Each team is limited to ten members. A photo of all team members must be submitted, along with a membership fee of two yuan and a deposit of five yuan. Members who have not registered or have not taken photos will not be allowed to participate. Violators will have their team's competition qualifications revoked. Furthermore, if they withdraw midway or are expelled from the association, the deposit will not be refunded, and the scores obtained in the competition will also be cancelled at the same time.

5. Time: The competition time is every Tuesday and Thursday from 5:00 PM, and Saturdays from 2:00 PM. Those who do not arrive at the venue five minutes after the scheduled time will be considered to have forfeited. If both parties do not arrive at the venue, it will be considered a forfeit for both parties. Those who forfeit twice will lose their competition qualifications, and the deposit will be confiscated.

6. Venue: Each competition will be held in the gymnasium of the China YMCA on Sichuan Road.

7. Grouping: Divided into two groups, business and academic. If there are many participating teams, they will be divided into more groups.

8. Postponement: In case of unavoidable circumstances that require postponement, the association must be notified and permission obtained three days before the competition date.

9. Uniforms: Teams without uniforms and players without numbers will not be allowed to participate in the competition.

10. Membership Card: Each team will be issued twelve membership cards by the association. The card is only valid for the dates when the team has competitions.

11. Awards: The association will present a silver shield to the champion of each group. 11. Protests: In the unfortunate event of a protest, it must be submitted in writing to the committee within two days of the incident, along with a deposit of five yuan. If the committee believes that the protest has sufficient grounds, the deposit will be refunded, otherwise it will be confiscated. However, the committee's decision is final and no further objections will be allowed.

Special Articles: New Trends in European Sports, Lecture by Cheng Dengke, Notes by Sha Zhongchi of Jiangnan Sports Teachers College

In our country, nothing is really on the right track, and sports are just one example. I remember when I first entered Berlin Sports University, the professor asked me about the overall organization and trends of sports in our country. I was stunned and couldn't answer. I, a member of the sports community, was in such a state, so it goes without saying for the rest of the working masses. Later, I promised that I would be able to provide a detailed reply when the Olympics were held in Berlin in 1936, but I had already realized my utter embarrassment and felt extremely ashamed. This was the greatest shame of my life. Looking at the progress of sports in European countries, it is flourishing, and the organization is truly meticulous and the facilities are well-equipped, which is quite astonishing. In addition to strengthening the body, the purpose is also to serve as a backup for the government. Sports are used to open up military training, instilling a unified spirit, sincere unity, and striving to enable the country or individuals to obtain the true benefits of sports. Therefore, every young person must receive sports training, military-style sports training, to increase their physical strength. Drawing lessons from the ancient Greek nation, the reason for their strength was the practice of reviving the past. Therefore, their slogan is "militarization of sports" and "sports militarization." The general outline of their sports facilities is described separately below:

Turkey: We all know that Turkey is an old country, the China of the West, which has always paid little attention to sports. As a result, the people's physical fitness is weak and their spirit is listless, and they are despised by the great powers. Now, since General Kemal came to power, he has implemented a revival movement, greatly innovating, and sending a large number of outstanding domestic talents and those interested in sports to study sports abroad, mostly to Germany. At the same time, he also hired German sports experts at great expense to design and establish large-scale national sports universities in the country in order to achieve his goal of strengthening the country and the race. I know that in the next World Games, the Turkish flag will surely give people a deep impression. Italy: Prime Minister Mussolini promotes sports with the spirit of Fascism, paying special attention to youth sports and children's sports, which is slightly different from Turkey. Mussolini recently established the Mussolini Sports University in Rome, which offers a doctorate in sports (Note by the reporter: no other country has this degree). The construction of the school is magnificent, with the ground paved with terrazzo and the walls built with marble, but it is not easily accessible to visitors. Without Mussolini's signature, any group or individual will be rejected. This is due to the ideology. When we went to visit the school, we first asked the German Ministry of Education to notify Mussolini, but we still didn't see the whole picture. Italy has a comprehensive standard and training for sports, and the uniforms of each young person are like those of the military. This is the trend of sports towards military training, which can be seen from this. Moreover, Mussolini is particularly strict in assessing sports teachers, because they should serve as role models and mentors for young people. The Italian slogan is "concentrate talents," "unite the whole," and "tie the country to sports," which is incomparable to the self-serving nature of our country's sports community.

Germany: All sports facilities in Germany are similar to those in Italy, but the national character is more vigorous than in Italy. Students from the Berlin National Sports University often exchange classes with students from the Rome Italian Sports University, but only a limited number of one or two people. In the past, foreign students coming to Germany to study at the National Sports University could account for half of the students, but the current government has issued an order to the school that foreign students are absolutely not allowed to be admitted in the future, implementing dictatorship. In short, everything in Germany imitates Italy, and the government organization is also like Italy, assimilated to Mussolini. The most fashionable cross-country running in Germany now is armed race walking, in other words, race walking in military uniform with guns and ammunition. Germany can train 100,000 junior officers every three years, all using sports as a fuse. Therefore, although Germany suffered a great deal in the European war, other countries still fear it like a tiger.

England: Witnessing the increasingly robust national character of Germany and Italy, England also realized the urgency and need for military sports, and is working hard to make progress every day, although it is slightly inferior to Germany and Italy. However, England uses extracurricular activities to give high-pressure methods, paying attention to youth sports and children's sports, sparing no effort.

France: France focuses on military sports and youth outdoor sports. Its open mountain and forest areas are equipped with bathrooms and other facilities for youth outdoor sports, and the government authorities give special preferential treatment to each ball team and track and field team when they go out to compete. No matter when and where, the transportation costs are reduced by half, and children are even free. Their attention to sports is very thoughtful.

Soviet Russia: Soviet Russia now has a meticulous plan for sports. The first step is to train a large number of primary school sports teachers, starting with elementary school students to lay the foundation. It also has large-scale public sports equipment, paying attention to the working masses, and especially promoting women's sports to strengthen the physical fitness of mothers. Therefore, in Europe, apart from Germany, Soviet Russia is the most outstanding. Summary: The new trend of sports in Europe, in addition to the above countries, is the same in Finland, Austria, Sweden, the Czech Republic, Yugoslavia, and other countries. They all pay attention to youth sports and children's sports. The governments of each country divide each person into three periods and determine the standard of sports performance. Each person sequentially reaches the performance within the time limit. At the age of eighteen, a sports examination is held. Those who fail are subject to legal restrictions and retrained. Governments at all levels also issue certificates and medals, and award prizes according to the level of achievement. The parents of those who win prizes even hang the prizes in the living room to show their glory. Adults and women can also participate, but are not restricted. In addition to the above, competitions such as target shooting, transporting ammunition, throwing hand grenades, digging trenches, and surveying geography are held every quarter. Various races are also conducted using the skirmish line method, and each person is instructed to run 100 meters or 200 meters without a target, knowing the location of the finish line. Moreover, each sports association is organized into a brigade to implement military training. In short, military affairs are incorporated into sports, so that everyone knows that to revitalize the country, it is necessary to hang up arms. This is the universally recognized purpose of the militarization of sports in Europe.

Finally, I offer some opinions to you all: (1) It is necessary to train sports teachers and lay the foundation for sports, and then use sports methods to revive the nation. (2) Sports should be democratized and popularized among farmers, workers, merchants, students, and soldiers, and lessons can be learned from Europe and the United States. (3) Our country's martial arts are excellent fighting skills, and should be explained with scientific methods to make them develop and expand. (4) Sports, martial arts, and military affairs should be integrated into a system of sports organization. (5) The Ministry of Education should have a sports inspector to specifically crack down on bad sports schools and reward successful sports schools, and to plan and integrate national sports affairs.

Gossip

Honored Account

— Wei Jing

The most headache-inducing thing must be "honored account," I think.

Rice shops, firewood shops, all have "honored accounts," department stores, newly established companies, also have "honored accounts," truly troublesome, unmanageable "honored accounts."

Germany, in the European war, owed the Allied countries a large war debt, to be repaid in installments, and it would take fifty years to clear that "honored account." This can be said to be a lifetime of slavery to the "honored account," and so they are preparing to throw the "honored account" into the furnace. But those demanding the "honored account" from Germany are mostly those who have received "honored accounts" from the United States, so if Germany were to really throw the "honored account" into the furnace, the United States, even if searching with lanterns in Europe, would find it difficult to stamp a "cleared" mark on the "honored account."

Germany ignoring the Allied countries' demands for the "honored account" would be one thing, but it is said that they are rummaging through old account books, preparing to send a "honored account" notice to France, truly audacious. And at the same time, Russia has also received several "honored accounts," look, in the Sino-Soviet negotiations over the Chinese Eastern Railway, didn't it once spread that the puppet Manchurian government demanded to use paper radishes as a toll, and investigate the old Russian banknotes stored among the people in Northeast China? The clamor for the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia has been going on for several years, and now it has finally been officially resumed. It is said that the United States' demand that Russia repay the old debts of the Tsarist era is also a major reason. It can be seen that all disputes are caused by the "honored account" acting up.

We Chinese are also frowning at the "honored account." The most famous is the Boxer Indemnity, which has been paid until now, with no hope of being cleared. There is also the Nishihara Loans, and although we have received the "honored account" notice, we don't know how to deal with it. The September 18th Incident, it is said, was Japan collecting the "honored account" of the Twenty-One Demands from us. But in the January 28th Incident, we suffered such a great loss for no reason, and until now, we are unable to send out this "honored account." In the Four Northeastern Provinces, our losses are even immeasurable, and to whom should we settle this "honored account"?

In the Library

— Huang Kewei

Every day, every day, taking advantage of my free time, I always go to the circulating library of this newspaper to read books; for a year, this library has simply become my own collection of books.

Standing in the elevator, slowly going up, the driver accurately asks: "Third floor?" I nod, and with a swish, it stops.

A few steps and I'm there, so I take a blue card with white characters as usual, and enter through the low door.

In the library, there is hardly anyone wearing fancy clothes, nor any modern girls; burying their heads, their eyes fixed on the books, are all poor friends bearing the burden of life. From this, it can be even clearer how many people there are who don't have money to study but are still working hard, right?

The exquisite reading room is filled with many people, but the air is so quiet and peaceful, upholding public morality, occasionally a few coughs and the rustling of newspapers.

The newspapers and magazines I want to read have all been taken by quick hands, so I have to hold my chin, my eyes drifting out the window, looking at the Jingwu Athletic Association across the street playing ping pong vigorously, looking at the white clouds in the sky, floating across the azure canopy. Waiting, waiting, a newly published magazine is in my hands, so I read quietly, each word flying into my brain to roll around, page by page; this is much better than watching that unconscious movie!

Every day, every day, I linger in the library, but I don't know if my own knowledge has improved a bit?

Wealthy Men and Fashionable Women

— Dao An

The term "talented men and beautiful women" is no longer applicable in today's increasingly progressive modernization. Look at the ideal partners of modern women, which one doesn't emphasize wealth? The ideal girlfriends of modern young men, which one doesn't emphasize fashion? In other words, women value wealth, and men value beauty. So "talented men and beautiful women" should now be changed to "wealthy men and fashionable women," which is more accurate. If you only have a belly full of learning but no money, then it is really impossible to get the favor of beauties. If women only have a beautiful appearance but no colorful and fashionable clothes, and have not been baptized by modernity, then how can they get the welcome of men.

Is money omnipotent? So women with weak will and admiring vanity are often tempted and hooked, and as a result, they are bound to be disappointed in love and ruined in reputation. But for women who cherish their purity, money cannot move their hearts, and temptations cannot change their minds.

Is money also the root of all evil? The love bought with money, which can make you pure and noble, is definitely not true love.

Small

— Hu Yanwen

The word "small" contains a bit of contempt, so adults scold children, opening their mouths with "little" ghost or "little" fellow, "little" Bi San.

But it is not always the case: modern women, if you tease them, saying that they will be the "small" mistress in a mansion in the future, then they will definitely raise their eyebrows, widen their almond eyes, and grit their silver teeth, cursing you to be killed a thousand times; if you praise their figure as delicate and "small", like a "small" angel, a cute "small" bird, then they will feign shyness and anger, sending you a charming wink. Isn't this a satisfying reward? As the West Chamber says, "How can it compare to that autumn wave at the moment of departure!" This charming wink will make your bones soft and muscles numb, which is truly a different feeling from cursing you to be killed a thousand times!

Japan is a "small" island, because it is so "small," so we people don't take it to heart; but Japan uses its somewhat "small" cleverness to work hard and finally occupy one of the positions of the great powers. It sent troops to seize our Three Northeastern Provinces, relying on its short and "small" elite soldiers, and helped the puppet country to establish itself. And China, with its large land and many soldiers, thinks its power is too "small" and dares not resist this short and "small" army.

The Nine Islands occupied by France are "small" islands too. Our aspirations, healthy and promising physique, under the leadership of the god of money, are consumed and exhausted. But money: doesn't come to entice you: doesn't lead you: isn't it you who goes to command money?

Is female beauty omnipotent? So young people with unsettled blood cannot withstand the alluring female beauty that is coquettish and charming. Those who are infatuated with the corners of qipao, begging for her pity and favor, have never been seen.

Is female beauty also the root of all evil? It can turn your hundred-refined steel into a finger-wrapping softness, and it can make you hypnotized, going east if she says east, going west if she says west: once she opens her mouth, except for not being able to get the stars in the sky, everything else can be done according to her orders: it can also make you enter a bewitched formation, confused and messed up. But female beauty: doesn't come to confuse you: doesn't tempt you: isn't it you who tempts them, worships them? This is called beauty does not bewitch people, people bewitch themselves.

Women's vanity is inherently strong, but to get lifelong happiness from vanity is probably a dream?

Men who are fickle, not hesitating to sacrifice money and spirit, even issuing a general mobilization order to the god of love, charging and fighting, going through fire and water, and going through all kinds of hardships. At the end of the day, they are bound to be defeated, and may even be forced to sign a treaty under the city. So to get a satisfactory and virtuous helper from the rouge team is probably not possible.

You must know that true love cannot be bought with money, because it is so "small," so we only argue with people a few words in words. People see that we are "small" and "small" spirited, and think that we can't do anything big, so they ignore us. The Chinese are too "small"-minded, afraid of quarreling with people and losing out, so they simply don't even make "small" noises!

The Chinese hang up a big signboard, but they all have "small" eyebrows, "small" eyes, "small" hearts, and are "small"-minded, so that the country's territory shrinks day by day, and in the international position, they can only be listed alongside those "small" countries in the colonies. Alas, China, there are no adults!

Fourth Company Commander of Northeast China

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Nineteen: Wanting to Leave, yet Reluctant to Leave, Remembering the Past in the Same Car; Half-Crying, Half-Laughing, Leaning on a Pillow, Sick in the Late Autumn

These words of Elder Zhao, on the surface, were explaining to himself, but in fact, he was explaining these words to everyone. Guizhi watched from the side, thinking, even a straightforward person like the old master is speaking in such roundabout ways, one can know his helplessness reached what extent. So she smiled at Elder Zhao: "I also say so. Whatever one does, one has to follow one's duty and follow along to do what one should do. Home is nothing, as long as things are accomplished, no matter how extravagant it is, the family will be able to be lively like that. This is my mind, but it is still considered small. Like Miss Huang, she is a big-minded, ambitious person, what country is going to perish, the donkey driver is responsible!" Elder Zhao laughed heartily upon hearing this. Huang Manying, who was sitting in the chair, had been keeping a straight face and looking down, not looking at anyone. At this time, hearing Guizhi saying several words wrong, she couldn't help but laugh. Elder Zhao said with a smile: "My eldest daughter, the country is going to perish, this is such a big thing, hastily asking the donkey driver to bear this responsibility, isn't this making things difficult? If you say these words to the donkey driver, he can truly say, what does it have to do with me, I can't manage it." Saying this, Huang Manying laughed again. Guizhi knew that she had said something wrong and should feel ashamed. But thinking that it was rare for Elder Zhao and Miss Huang to laugh so heartily, she said: "Yo! Miss Huang, didn't you tell me like this? How come when we say it, it provokes you to laugh so heartily?" Huang Manying said with a smile: "How do you plan to ask the donkey driver to bear the responsibility of the country's perishing?" Jiang Shi stood on the side, not knowing what kind of mystery they were talking about. But seeing them laughing like this, it was certainly a funny thing, so she naturally echoed them and laughed together. Because of this big laugh, a lot of sadness was reduced for everyone. Elder Zhao's concern that the Yang family mother and daughter would not be happy was also relieved. (246)

Social Snapshot

The Charge Horn of Crying

— Zhuo

Mr. Zhu Qian wrote an article "General Mobilization of Laughter," which has a lot of humor. In the various jokes, it seems that one can smell the crying of the insiders, which is especially commendable! This youngster is wary of the accusation of writing a sequel. I have scribbled a "Charge Horn of Crying." If the reader can find some laughs in this article, it is an extra gift.

Crying in the Sedan Chair In our Ningbo customs, when a woman is married, the family hires a sedan chair to bring the bride home. When picking up the bride, after the daughter bids farewell to the elders, when she is about to get into the sedan chair, she must face her mother and cry a song about getting into the sedan chair. The lyrics are readily available, and the villagers circulate them very widely. Little girls of five or six years old can learn to cry it in a drawn-out voice. The elders not only do not forbid it, but also praise: "Crying well! Our daughter is really good!" They don't think it's inauspicious, the more sad the crying, the more they think it's auspicious! The original meaning of the daughter crying goodbye is completely lost. On this day, the daughter also tries her best to cry out the sedan chair song she has practiced for more than ten years, word by word, so that everyone who comes to listen to the song from relatives, friends, and neighbors is satisfied and returns, then her life will be well-received!

The Authority of the Police Three or five rickshaws, because they can't find customers, the rickshaw pullers idly cross their legs and hang their hands on the rickshaw shafts, lingering at the end of the street. The policeman on duty here sees this and walks over, raising the baton in his hand and banging it randomly on the rickshaw canopies. Immediately, everyone pulls their rickshaws and flees. The last rickshaw puller, caught off guard, gets hit on the shoulder, pulls the empty rickshaw and barely escapes a few steps, presumably in unbearable pain. He loses his grip and the rickshaw shaft he was holding falls to the ground. The policeman misunderstands that he is not obeying his actions and is expressing anger, and chases after him, snatching a rickshaw cushion. The rickshaw puller, as usual, begs and kowtows, performing a Chinese drama. The policeman, because of his position, always occupies the superior position, so he is as arrogant as the emperor. No matter how many times you kowtow, or how many times you call him "Police Officer," he turns a deaf ear to everything! At this time, a inspector wearing a Zhongshan suit happens to arrive, inquires about what happened, and is furious! The rickshaw puller takes off his coat, revealing a bloodstain as thick as a chrysanthemum on his shoulder. The inspector, seeing this, is even more enraged and severely reprimands the police officer. He writes a line in the police officer's personal investigation diary, comforts the rickshaw puller a few words, orders the return of the rickshaw cushion, and lets the rickshaw puller pull his rickshaw and leave with tears in his eyes before leaving himself. At this time, the authority of the police officer has been stripped away, he stares bitterly at the inspector's back, with a crying face that is difficult to describe; this face expresses the life of "the big eats the small"!

Wedding Night On the wedding night, the bride cries sadly. The groom can't bear it, intending to persuade her to stop, but suddenly finds himself at a loss for words. After a while, the bride continues to cry sadly, and after a long time, the bride actually cries even more vigorously! The groom has to summon his courage and say, "Don't cry, crying is very bad for your body and mind! And it's not suitable for today!" The bride doesn't seem to hear and continues to cry loudly. The groom hesitates for a while and says again, "Don't cry! Are you thinking of your mother? But you have to understand: your mother doesn't allow you to cry like this either!" The bride pauses and starts crying again. The groom is disinterested in the fun, and angrily says, "Don't cry, I hate people crying the most, you know?" The bride listens and stops crying, and there is a smile on her face, which surprises the groom. He inadvertently asks the reason, and the bride smiles coquettishly, "My mother told me: if you like to laugh, I should cater to you and laugh; if you want me to cry, I have to obey and cry loudly. I knew you didn't like crying, so I wouldn't shed tears!"

Securities Short Covering Turns into Selling, Irresistible Trend, Public Debt New Low Prices Emerge One After Another, |Longs Down 2.3 Yuan, Shorts Down Around 1 Yuan|

Yesterday, due to the Minbian Incident at the Chinese Securities Exchange and the central government's severe response, threatening military force, the general mood was extremely panicked. Longs were almost entirely liquidated, and retail investors mostly turned short. The situation was on the verge of a steep decline. The Minbian was in the planning stage, with widespread connections and a large scope, but due to disagreements on the main objectives, most had separated. They launched the revolt as a desperate measure, but their actions were reckless. Therefore, although Fujian Province claimed independence, it was essentially isolated. Judging from military, financial, geographical, personnel, it should not be difficult to suppress. The fluctuations of the public debt market were controlled by a few major players. Retail investors frantically sold off, providing an opportunity for major players to buy in. In the current situation, retail investors have all turned short, and a rebound is not far off. Yesterday morning, after the Minbian Incident broke out, various gangs scrambled to sell off. Most of the recent longs had already capitulated. The downsizing bonds plunged 1.5 yuan, retreating to the 60 yuan mark, and the rest also fell by around 1 yuan. In the second session, the situation was slightly confusing. Generally speaking, the middle one to three types were still slightly firm by 0.1 to 0.2 yuan, while the leading and trailing types continued to fall by several points. New low prices were repeatedly discovered, indicating that there were still many speculators. In the afternoon session, which started after 6 pm, the news was gloomy and there were no major changes. Longs were still rolling over contracts. Near-term downsizing bonds were weaker, while long-dated bonds were firmer. The 19th-issue Guanshan bonds were generally up 0.2 to 0.3 yuan, and the 20th-issue for this month was also up 0.3 yuan. Long-dated contracts were down 0.2 yuan. This was because No. 50 was determined to suppress small market participants, so the price was forcibly reduced from 43.8 yuan to 42.8 yuan, a sharp drop of 1 yuan. However, due to the continued influx of buyers, it rebounded to 43.3 yuan, showing the intensity of the competition. It can also be seen that the shorts were running out of steam. In the later types, they were gradually strengthening, and the sudden surge of 0.8 yuan in gold shorts can be used to summarize the rest. As a result, the market prices were down 2.3 yuan for the most part and down around 1 yuan for the least. Generally speaking, near-term contracts were down more, while long-dated contracts were down less. This was entirely due to longs rolling over contracts. The total trading volume was estimated to be around 30 million yuan for the three sessions.

Yarn and Cotton, Yarn and Cotton Still Show a Weak Trend

The yarn market is trending down, showing weakness. Free Talk

A Realistic Understanding (Part 2)

— Shi Heng

But when Turgenev extracted this "prototype" from reality, the artist Turgenev was acting as a prophet. Whether he could make this "prototype" grow and transform from a prophet into an artist completely depended on his artistic expression. In my observation, Turgenev achieved this. Conversely, Arkady Averchenko, the author of "Sanin," was also a prophet, but his prediction was incorrect. Of course, Averchenko himself believed that he had extracted something similar to a "prototype" from reality before he started writing, but unfortunately, his understanding of reality was incorrect. His "Sanin" would never appear in the "new era," and Averchenko, who transformed from a prophet into an artist, showed too many deficiencies in his talent. His artistic expression was even more incorrect than his prediction. Therefore, "Sanin," no matter how much it angered society at the time of its publication, was a complete failure.

I have pointed out that Sanin is not the author but an ideal character completely opposed to the author, but in "Sanin" we can see the shadow of the author, which is the young Yuri, who was paralyzed in all his actions by the evils of education and eventually died by suicide. His character is completely opposite to Sanin's. Sanin is an excessively strong person, while Yuri is an excessively weak person, but both are equally unreal. Just as the author gave Sanin a superior condition to make him a hero, the author gave Yuri all the humble conditions to make him a hesitant person without faith or action. The author not only mocks him implicitly everywhere but even has Sanin say such words on Yuri's grave: "Now there is one less mediocre person in the world!" How can "Sanin," which is similar to the production method of Chinese novels, become a book of realistic expression art!

But even if we step back, if the author of "Sanin" had extracted the "prototype" of reality in the same way as the author of "Fathers and Sons," could his artistic expression have achieved the same success as Turgenev's? I can answer without a doubt that it was absolutely impossible. If a writer uses the form of essay explanation, only a correct understanding of reality or sufficient, at most, clear and smooth writing is enough. But if writing a novel, drama, or poem that is not entirely logical, then more artistic production talent and effort are necessary, and the art that Averchenko showed in "Sanin" was indeed lacking too much. In this short essay, I only want to make readers understand and agree with me on one point, which is to illustrate that the understanding of reality is inextricably linked to the correct expression of art. The saying of a certain gentleman that only the former can complete the production of art is wrong in any case. Moreover, if a writer has a correct understanding of reality but no correct expression of art, then even the part of his understanding will be destroyed.

What is "Selected Studies?"

— Bu Dian

The evil of Selected Studies still holds great power. Even famous contemporary writers have been bewitched by it, as "Free Talk" has already discussed in detail.

What is Selected Studies? We don't need to ask this foolish question at first. But it is not impossible to discuss it from the perspective of literary historians. I am using old stories and clichés, and unfortunately, there is no "new knowledge" for new people to draw upon, which is what I should apologize for.

During the Sui and Tang dynasties, there was a person named Cao Xian who was proficient in the textual studies of various schools. Since the Han dynasty, the ancient script of Du Lin and Wei Hong had been lost, but Cao Xian revived this learning. Emperor Taizong of Tang once encountered difficult words while reading, and he recorded the words that were missing from the dictionaries and asked Cao Xian about them. Cao Xian provided phonetic and explanatory annotations for all of them, along with clear citations, which greatly impressed Emperor Taizong. He was a highly respected scholar of phonology and lexicography at the time, holding the high position of reading advisor to the emperor at the old age of one hundred years. His Annotations on the Literary Selections was highly valued at the time. Initially, scholars of Literary Selections in the Jianghuai region based their studies on Cao Xian. Later, Xu Yan, Li Shan, and Gongsun Luo successively taught Literary Selections, and their scholarship flourished in the world. Thus, Selected Studies began during the Sui and Tang dynasties and flourished in the early Tang dynasty, with Cao Xian as the founding master of this learning. Du Fu wrote in a poem, "Continuing to have my son recite the Literary Selections," and "Also instructing his son to thoroughly understand the principles of the Literary Selections," indicating that Selected Studies became a distinct school of thought throughout the Tang dynasty.

During the Five Dynasties period, a Jinshi examination in Jiangnan required the writing of a poem on "Heavenly Rooster Playing with Gentle Breeze." When asked about the two Heavenly Roosters in Erya, the presiding examiner, Zhang Bi, was also proficient in Selected Studies. Therefore, there is a saying: "If one understands Literary Selections thoroughly, half of the scholars will succeed." After the Xining and Yuanfeng eras, scholars focused on pedantically discussing the classics, and Selected Studies fell into decline. In times when scholars were selected based on poetry and fu, Selected Studies flourished, while in times when scholars were selected based on Confucian exegesis and the eight-legged essay, Selected Studies declined. Today, there is also the Hall of Talents, and based on the trend of selecting scholars and evaluating their essays, one can also predict the rise and fall of Selected Studies.

Chrysanthemum

— Zhou Lengjia

I walked alone on Avenue Joffre, standing in front of a flower shop.

Chrysanthemums were in full bloom. In the glass window, various kinds of flowers were displayed, pinkish-white, light purple, goose-yellow, dark green, arranged in rows on the shelves. It unconsciously evokes a sense of beauty in people who see them.

A wooden tag was hanging on the stem of each flower. I don't know which elegant person named them: Golden Hook, Crab Claw, Night Fragrance, Beauty Rainbow, Eastern Fence Competing for Freshness, Old Gardener's Autumn Appearance, from two characters to four characters. It is a pity that these chrysanthemums are being treated as commercial goods here. Hanging wooden tags on them makes them seem out of place. Among all the flowers, I love chrysanthemums the most. This love is not simply for their color and fragrance, like those old-fashioned people. It is because their spirit of pride and unyieldingness is very much like that of a group of people who dedicate themselves to truth and never repent until death. And these people are the ones I respect the most.

I stood in front of the flower shop, looking at those flowers. Suddenly, I thought of my home, my desk, and that there were still some decorations missing on the window sill in front of my desk. I began to have an idea that I wanted to buy two pots of flowers to take home.

After many comparisons and selections, I finally chose two identical pots of flowers, wrote down an address, and asked the shop people to send them over to me.

When I returned home from outside, the chrysanthemums had already arrived before me and were placed on the window sill of my desk. The light purple flowers stood proudly, as if smiling at me.

I sat silently, admiring the posture of the flowers. Every day, I have such a quiet realm. This is my time for spiritual enjoyment. During this time, I have no intentions, no hopes, and not even any memories.

I only think of a poem, the famous line of the Japanese poet Matsuo Basho: The sound of the water when a little frog jumps into the desolate old pond.

But now, I no longer think of that poem. I only face the two pots of chrysanthemums. Chrysanthemums, like that poem, are full of refreshing charm and can also give me spiritual happiness.

"Not disliking the old gardener's autumn appearance as bland, only loving the fragrance of yellow flowers in their late bloom," I murmured softly, feeling comfortable in body and mind. I really have some petty-bourgeois temperament. However, the whip of real life is spurring me on. I can't always enjoy that pure happiness. I don't even have time to water the flowers and move the flower pots.

Every night, I move the flower pots to the courtyard to receive the dew, and in the morning, I move them back and place them on the window. These are all my wife's work. I am just an existing enjoyer.

My wife also has a chrysanthemum addiction like me, although her addiction is slightly different from mine. She simply likes to watch them for fun.

One day, my wife went back to her mother's home. These chrysanthemums were taken care of by me.

I poured some water into the pot but forgot to move the pot into the courtyard.

That night, I had a very strange dream: It was as if I had begun to walk into a chrysanthemum exhibition, and suddenly, that chrysanthemum exhibition turned into a vast execution ground, and those chrysanthemums had all turned into people being executed. It seemed that these people being executed were all familiar friends of mine, and then suddenly there were intermittent gunshots.

I woke up abruptly. It was not yet dawn. When I walked to the window to look, both pots of chrysanthemums had completely withered. The light purple petals were scattered in the pot, on the window, and on my desk. The color was just like congealed fresh blood.

My heart was beating slightly. I solemnly gathered the petals, hid them in a paper bag, carried them to the courtyard, dug a pit, and buried them.

Like a loving mother offering her only beloved son, I was doing my burial work with the same devout attitude.

Literary Miscellany

— Meng Yuan

Bored in illness, I read Hu Shih's "Forty Self-Narration," the autobiography of a hero who descended from heaven. In the chapter "How I Went Abroad," he narrated the tide of the Chinese Public School at that time, the students' efforts to fight for freedom. He sent this original manuscript to his classmate Wang Jingfang at that time. Wang replied, "I was the most vocal person who opposed abolishing the rules at the beginning, but today, I really can't answer how much harm the abolishing the rules will cause to Chinese students. You were the most vocal person who opposed the Chinese Public School at that time. Seeing your article, the observations of the present and the past are very different. I think that young people's reason is suppressed by emotional impulses, and most of the trends in Chinese schools are due to this reason. One less trend in school means one more achievement. I hope you pay attention to correcting this malpractice." Dr. Hu then added that I agree with this statement, but I want to add one sentence: The trends in schools are not entirely due to young people's reason being suppressed by emotions. Among them, it is often because middle-aged people and young people have equally lost the ability to use reason. It is unfair to blame young people alone. The recent trends in the Chinese Public School are good examples.

One can see the changes in a person's thoughts and opinions here. Dr. Hu's meaning is very clear. At first, fighting for freedom was felt to be very meaningful, but now, it is "no big deal". Mr. Wang, one of the "strong generals," thought after the fact that the mistake was on his own side, and that fighting for freedom at that time was not right, advocating "one less trend, more achievements". Dr. Hu, another "strong general," in addition to accepting his opinion, thought that it was somewhat "inappropriate" to assign the responsibility to young people alone, so he said, "Middle-aged people and young people have equally lost the ability to use reason." Why has our doctor had such a change in his understanding of events? I say, this is why Hu Shih is Hu Shih (this "Hu Shih" should be translated as "Where are you going"). In the beginning, Dr. Hu and others withdrew from the Chinese Public School due to the trend and established the New Chinese Public School. In the end, because they could not sustain it, they returned to the old Chinese Public School under the cover of mediation. Although the doctor also felt a little "difficult," writing poems with complaints such as "There should be a feeling of the end of the world, do not forget the alliance under the city," but surrender and capitulation are ultimately surrender and capitulation. Therefore, later, a certain general opposed the vernacular, but could offer five thousand gold as a birthday gift to the "Ancestor of the Vernacular," in the eyes of people with "historical addiction and textual research addiction," Dr. Hu's actions over the years are like this.

Two Brothers (36)

— Written by Maupassant, Translated by Li Weike

Mr. Roland raised his head, searching in his memory,

"Wait a minute, I don't remember very well. This matter has been so long ago, ah! That's right, I remember. Your mother met him in the store, didn't she, Louise? He came to the store to order a few things at that time, and then he often came. He was just our customer at first, and later became a friend."

Pierre was eating a bowl of beans. He picked them up one by one with the tip of his fork, as if stringing the beans on it, and said, "When did this friendship begin?"

Roland thought again, but couldn't remember at all. He turned to his wife's memory for help,

"In that year, let's think about it, Louise? You must not have forgotten, your memory is so good. Think about it, it was in...in...in eighteen hundred and fifty-five or fifty-six? ... Hey, think about it, I'm sure you remember more clearly than I do." She really thought for a moment, and then said in a certain and calm voice,

"It was in eighteen hundred and fifty-eight. Pierre was only three years old at that time. I believe I haven't misremembered, because Pierre was suffering from scarlet fever that year, and although our friendship with Marais was still very shallow at that time, he helped us a lot." Roland exclaimed,

"That's true, that's true, he was simply admirable at that time. Your mother was so exhausted by you, and I had to take care of the store's business, so he went to the pharmacist to get medicine for you. He was really a kind-hearted person. And when you fully recovered, you don't know how happy he was and how he hugged and kissed you. We became good friends from this time." Then this sudden, fierce thought, like a bullet that pierced and cracked people,窜進了 Pierre's soul: "Since he met me first, took care of me like this, since he liked me and kissed me like that, since I was the reason he made friends with my parents, why did he leave all his property to my brother and not give me any?"

He no longer asked questions. He was now quietly silent, and it would be more accurate to say that he was burying his head in consideration rather than imagining something. In this silence, he maintained a new and not very clear concern, a new and painful source of secrecy. He left early and wandered the streets again. The street was shrouded in fog, which made the night heavy, dark, and nauseating. It was simply like an infectious smoke falling on the ground. We could see this smoke flowing in front of the gas lamps, which sometimes seemed to be extinguished by it. The stones paved on the street became slippery, like an icy night, and all the stenches, the恶臭 of cellars, caves, sewers, poor kitchens, were mixed in the恶臭 of this飘流 fog, as if they came out of the belly of those houses.

Pierre bent his back, put his hands in his pockets. He didn't want to stay outside when it was so cold. He walked to the Marosco's house. The old pharmacist was always dozing under the gas lamp, watching the store for himself. When he recognized Pierre, who he loved with the faithful love of a dog, he quickly cheered up, ran to find two cups and brought the raspberry wine. "How about it! How far has your sweet wine been promoted?" the doctor asked.

Talk

Diagnosis and Treatment of Degenerative Disease

— Lizhai

In the era of raging storms and the thorny road ahead for Europe, many young people became "ill" after experiencing one or more setbacks in their lives. If the patient really consulted a hospital or a licensed doctor, the symptoms they described would be nothing more than: headache, back pain, neurasthenia, weakness in the limbs, lethargy, frequent dreams, insomnia, etc. And the most that doctors could do to help him was to give him a few injections to replenish blood and nourish the brain, tell him to eat more eggs, milk, and greens, and tell him to "rest and recuperate." However, on the other hand, leaving aside the routine diagnostic procedures such as testing body temperature, pulse, blood, and excrement, we find in the lifestyles of many young people a very common disease that is "deeply ingrained" and slightly "infectious." The most appropriate name for this disease is "Degenerative Disease" or "Romantic Disease."

For the time being, I will imitate the routine procedures of real doctors and masters. Here, I will also boldly diagnose, find the source, and prescribe a prescription for young people suffering from degenerative disease.

First of all, in terms of symptoms, degenerative disease has the following three special signs: First, spiritual distortion. Patients with degenerative disease are usually unable to cheer up their spirits, but at the same time, they constantly waste their energy in a life of "groaning without illness." These people often put on a depressed and melancholy face of "a heartbroken person has other feelings," adapting to all objective natural and human problems with the mood of grieving for autumn and cherishing spring, crying for flowers and mourning the moon. What he most hopes for is "May the flowers always be beautiful, the moon always be round, people always live long, and the years always be abundant," but the development of reality is precisely the opposite of his hopes. So, he can't help but be overcome with grief! The subjective archetype of male degenerative disease sufferers is people like Jia Changsha and Li Changji, and the subjective "model" of female degenerative disease sufferers is Lin Daiyu! These people often seem to have the sorrows of a country broken, a family destroyed, and a vast life, but they are indifferent to the splitting of the four northeastern provinces and the large-scale attacks of imperialism. Second, sensual pleasure. "Life is like a dream, how much happiness can there be?" is the motto that degenerative disease sufferers unanimously rejoice in: "Pure wine and women, fearing that they will not be available," is the lifestyle practiced by most degenerative disease sufferers. He indulges in gambling at the "turntable," dances in the dance hall until "unaware of the dawn in the east," buys a dollar's worth of "Yun Gao" to smoke himself into a daze, and various other pleasure methods aimed at exchanging temporary or momentary anesthesia and stimulation of nerves and senses. In the life of every degenerative disease sufferer, there is one or "all-around" "tireless enjoyment" in any aspect. Third, "don't care about tomorrow" and dissatisfaction with everything. Self-anesthesia and sensual pleasure are themselves the second step in the development of "don't care about tomorrow." "Get drunk today if you have wine today" and "Tonight we can only talk about the wind and the moon" are even more "heretical mantras" often recited by many degenerates when "forgetting their worries with joy." Secondly, degenerative disease sufferers almost always take a negative or "scornful" attitude towards everything. For example, although he himself is being attacked by sexual hunger, but when he sees others in love, he piously reprimands them as "impulses of animal lust"; when he sees people looking for a job, he sarcastically calls them "slaves of life"; when talking about politics, he indiscriminately dismisses them as "leading beasts to eat people"; when talking about political parties, his opinion is: The word "party" contains "still" and "black", how can there be good ones? When talking about resisting Japan and opposing imperialism, they think it is "wanting to show off" or "being used by others". In short, everything in the eyes of degenerative disease sufferers is "stupid" and "terrible". However, degenerates themselves never want to think about, say, or do things that are "not stupid" or "not terrible"! Patients with degenerative disease invariably seek anesthesia and stimulation, but anesthesia and stimulation can only temporarily obscure reality for him. As a result, when the anesthetic properties disappear, he is still cruelly whipped by the pressure of reality. Therefore, the degenerative disease itself is a kind of chronic suicide, and the sudden and dramatic changes in degenerative disease often develop into actual suicide.

Secondly, we trace the source of degenerative disease. The objective reason, of course, is that the semi-colonial social economy is increasingly bankrupt and the long-term turmoil and unrest in the whole of China give young people too many opportunities to encounter obstacles. The subjective reason is that the degenerative disease patient himself does not have enough understanding of the problems of life and society and lacks the courage to grasp reality and struggle hard.

Finally, I have to prescribe a "self-healing" "prescription" for friends suffering from degenerative disease:

First, use all the spirit of groaning without illness and the sigh of "talented people (or "beautiful women") have a short life" on analyzing problems and dealing with problems. Basically, you must recognize that in this world that you think is boring, you still have to continue to live in most cases. Since you want to live, you must make life richer and more reasonable.

Second, in terms of personal daily life, it must be made very tight and orderly. In terms of the relationship between people, you must make yourself more in contact with the masses, from monotonous to collectivized or massified. Because the deep penetration of people in degenerative disease often comes from the "leisure" and loneliness of life.

Third, open your eyes, recognize the era and environment you are in, and establish your own fighting outlook on life from a materialist worldview and social outlook.

This world simply does not have surplus rice and bread to feed many degenerates or no reserves. Therefore, I advise all degenerates: "Quickly turn back!"

Toilet

— Guanghan

The toilet is a place that doesn't make people very happy, but you have to approach it from time to time. When a person arrives in the toilet, it is indeed very boring, not as exciting as going to the theater or a restaurant; but a kind of leisurely and comfortable attitude is enough to refresh one's spirits. We are busy all day long for life and career, so busy that we can't get away; once we step into the toilet, our body and mind are relaxed for the most part, and we can immediately get a few minutes of peace and quiet. Or hold a cigarette in your mouth, slowly inhale and exhale, and stare intently at the ever-changing smoke rings in front of you. Or hold your head in both hands, carefully savoring the sweet aftertaste of the past. In this state, no matter how unhappy you are, you have to temporarily throw away all the pain in the world.

If you are willing to pay attention and observe quietly, in the toilet, we can always discover many strange and bizarre scenes, which will make a smile float on the corner of your mouth. Works of art are often appreciated. An extremely simple turtle composed of a few strokes, or three or five strangely shaped human figures, and vulgar sentences such as "A person is at the guest's center, the home is at the heart," these are the masterpieces of several unknown painters and poets. "Amu is being detained," "Adai eats rice and dung," the surrounding whitewashed walls have become bulletin boards for children to attack each other, which is truly beautiful and full of fun! Not only that, in recent years, the toilet has also become a place for writing slogans. The competition of doctrines has even reached the toilet, which is quite peculiar! Slogans such as "Down with the ×× Party", "Long live ××ism", and "Support the ×× Government" are everywhere. This is another achievement of a group of unknown revolutionary activists. These forms can be grabbed as good tricks for us to pass the time.

As for a generation of studious bookworms, they can also make great efforts by taking advantage of the time they spend in the toilet; holding a book in their hands, concentrating and reading one word after another. This is also a way to burn the midnight oil, and the benefits should be considerable. It is said that several famous Chinese and foreign scholars obtained part of their knowledge from the toilet.

Some people, when they meet familiar friends in the toilet, they have to talk loudly and eloquently. The topics of conversation here are very casual and broad, sometimes starting from pulling the flush and talking all the way to issues such as eating, love, politics, international affairs, life and death.

There is also a kind of person who can sleep soundly in the toilet. But this is very dangerous, if you fall down, it's no joke!
