Behind Vanity

— Xiaoying

It is said that a monk in Jiaoshan, Zhenjiang, once analyzed the busyness of the world, believing that the motivation lies in fame and fortune, and the two are parallel and diverge. However, if we further investigate the motivation for people's pursuit of fame, there are no Yi and Qi who starved to death in Shouyang Mountain in this world. As for the so-called famous officials and great men, who would dare to say that they are not engaging in the mutual exploitation of interests?

Mr. Jiyun discussed vanity in this publication yesterday, attributing all the evils in the world to vanity, believing that if people did not embrace vanity and paid attention to practical benefits and utilitarianism, the world would be at peace. However, this may be too optimistic! Most people in the world wear plain clothes and eat simple food, but their actions are still the same set of pursuing selfishness and self-interest. In addition to increasing a group of true villains who are unwilling to contribute even a hair, only hypocrites are eliminated, and what benefit does it bring to the world?

Naturally, Mr. Jiyun's premise is this: because of vanity, expenditures are large; because expenditures are large, they commit crimes and collect money, leading to self-harm and harm to others. If we ask further, why be vain? That is definitely not just because they want to make their wives and concubines proud, or sit in a black-plated car and watch pedestrians. The motivation is not just reversing the cause and effect, it is precisely for the sake of committing crimes. Tell Mr. Jiyun! It is definitely not vanity that drives unscrupulous merchants. However, those unscrupulous merchants who desperately pursue the vanity of a piece of empty committee title are actually trying to cover themselves up with some so-called social status!

Humans are the spirit of all things, especially in the so-called bad aspects. Every move, every smile, in this commodified stage of real society, flirting and showing off is not limited to prostitutes who are despised. It can even be said that everyone has become a prostitute. The so-called "speak human language to people, speak ghost language to ghosts" in the philosophy of life, is it not the meaning of a shallow smile by the wine pot?

The author is not a so-called pessimistic person who hates the world, but wants to expose the overly optimistic attitude of reforming the heart and improving society, so he believes that the new advice to the world to not have vanity, without understanding what is behind vanity, is a futile thing. This is an inevitable fact. It is as fruitless to preach frugality to celebrities as it is to preach not killing to tigers. Maybe they will even laugh at you for being too naive! "How can I be fond of vanity? I have no choice!" This sentence is also a bit of truth.

In this era, it is absolutely impossible to dream of Peach Blossom Spring again. No one can show the temperament of not bending the waist for five pecks of rice. Rice cannot be obtained more and more like air. Even if you go your own way, people only recognize clothes and hats and not people. Morality cannot be practiced without skills, and vanity has long been regarded as a great skill.

I oppose vanity, and I will never advocate vanity. However, understanding what is behind vanity, I know that abandoning the root and pursuing the branches will not only fail to get rid of vanity, but also cause you to run into walls. To put it in a fashionable way, this is related to the fundamental problem.

Seeking Benevolence and Obtaining Benevolence, What is There to Complain About?"

— Qiongsheng

China has always given praise to the tragic ending of heroes and righteous people since ancient times, but I don't understand it.

For example, Taishi Gong's Biography of Boyi says: "Boyi and Shuqi were the two sons of the monarch of Guzhu. The father wanted to establish Shuqi. When the father died, Shuqi gave way to Boyi. Boyi said, 'It is the father's order,' and then fled away. Shuqi also refused to be established and fled. The people of the country established the middle son. Then Boyi and Shuqi heard that Xibo Chang was good at supporting the elderly, and went to return to him. When they arrived, Xibo died, and King Wu carried a wooden tablet and called himself King Wen, and attacked Zhou to the east. Boyi and Shuqi knocked on the horse and advised him, saying: 'Is it filial to not bury the father when he dies and use weapons of war? Is it benevolent to kill the ruler with a subject?'...After King Wu had pacified the Yin chaos, the world followed Zhou, but Boyi and Shuqi were ashamed of it, and righteously refused to eat Zhou millet, hid in Shouyang Mountain, picked weeds and ate them, and starved to death." Reading this passage, at least it is indignant and laments that Boyi and Shuqi died unjustly. They didn't want to be good emperors, ran away to join King Wu, who was not very bright, and eventually starved to death. However, Confucius, who "considered himself benevolent and righteous," greatly praised them, saying: "Boyi and Shuqi did not remember old evils, and resentment was therefore rare. Seeking benevolence and obtaining benevolence, what is there to complain about?" These words came from the mouth of Confucius, who traveled around the countries like the current "national heroes," "celebrities," and "masters," and everywhere people held welcome meetings and donated money. I think he is extremely sarcastic and cold-blooded!

Just as Confucius' "benevolence, righteousness, and morality" still dominate people's hearts and are considered the "national character" of China, his sarcastic and cold-blooded attitude has also been maintained to this day. Jiang Minsheng fought bloodily with the enemy for many years, and now has to engage in the industry of wiping shoes for a living. Liang Tongfang, as a leader of an anti-Japanese army, actually lives by walking with people. Resisters are like this, and non-resisters are like that. No matter what, it is regrettable, but some people praise it as a "glorious ending," a "self-reliant" "heroic quality," which has the same meaning as sitting next to an electric stove in winter and watching the laborers struggling in the cold wind on the street, and praising them for having a "spirit of enduring hardship."

But then again, saying this does not mean that "anti-Japanese heroes" must be commanders-in-chief, commanders, or chairmen, and must be so before they are happy. Boyi and Shuqi valued etiquette and lightness and had their own "seeking benevolence and obtaining benevolence" intention, which does not need to be criticized. However, there are those who "reside in benevolence and do not give way," such as the warlord Liu Bei, who seized Xichuan, and they feel that Boyi and Shuqi were too stupid and should not have been. King Wu's replacing Zhou was really "using violence to replace violence." As a result, resisting by refusing to eat Zhou millet and starving to death in Shouyang was an even more sinful passive attitude. When the Northeast Volunteer Army rose up, from fundraising teams and support associations to hundreds of thousands of "destroying homes and contributing to the disaster," gathering small amounts to make a fur coat was quite a large number. However, there were many people who were both "famous" and "substantial" as "patriots who saved the country." This was originally like speculation in the stock exchange. Jiang Minsheng and Liang Tongfang may not have understood this at that time, which led to their "exhaustion," and they could not travel to Western Europe after the "anti-Japanese war was successful." Returning home to visit mountains and scenic spots amid a crowd of welcomes is enough to show that they are not very clever. Clever people will say that stupid people are "commendable for their loyalty and bravery." Therefore, people who have made a fortune in the "anti-Japanese" stock exchange, with their pockets full, said to Jiang Minsheng and Liang Tongfang in a tone that superficially praised but was actually sarcastic and cold-blooded, imitating "seeking benevolence and obtaining benevolence, what is there to complain about?": "Everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world. When the country is in trouble, stand up and act as a bulwark. Once the disaster is removed, remove the armor and return to the fields, shining shoes is a profession, pulling a rickshaw is a profession, labor is sacred, what is there to be humiliated about, not taking credit, not seeking reward, this is the true color of a hero." It is highly doubtful whether the disaster has been removed. Whether the action of "everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world" has been treated as goods and is being traded on the "anti-Japanese" stock exchange must be carefully considered. As for saying that not seeking reward or taking credit is the true color of a hero, Jiang and Liang must have hidden themselves in Shouyang Mountain and picked weeds to eat in order to be the most "noble" when they saw the current national territory shrinking and instead talked about friendship! However, that would be too stupid.

In this society where everything has been commodified, the "heroic" cause of loving the country and "resisting Japan" cannot escape this law. The various forms of saving the country that are still going on now show this sign. Many truly "everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world" people are sold out under this form. Some "heroes" who are both "famous" and "substantial" praise fools with grand-sounding "noble personalities" and wag their seductive tongues. Yes, in order to avoid the general public from becoming "indignant," the more people who righteously refuse to eat Zhou millet and starve to death in Shouyang, the better. However, there are few such people in China. Therefore, the saying of praising fools as "commendable for their loyalty and bravery" is just right. Jiang Minsheng and Liang Tongfang are, after all, heroic qualities, "seeking benevolence and obtaining benevolence, what is there to complain about?"

However, I feel that it is extremely sarcastic and cold-blooded.

Fiction

Fragments of Childhood Memories (10)

— Liehuo

After waiting for a quarter of an hour, I finally went to the front of the cattle pen with a sad face, staring blankly at a very large golden-yellow bull. My mother saw that I hadn't started yet and hurried forward, "The sun has already come out of the mountains, why aren't you leading the cow away? Good boy, listen to me, go! When you come back, I'll give you a bowl of egg fried rice. Your fourth brother didn't have this kind of blessing when he herded cows. Go quickly!" My mother said a lot of words early in the morning, but they couldn't match the pleasantness of the sentence "When you come back, I'll give you a bowl of egg fried rice." I panicked. Suddenly, half of his head appeared on the bottom of the pond, and I couldn't help laughing. Then he drew a few circles in the center of the pond and told me to go into the water. I went into the water. Then he taught me a few swimming poses: "Close your mouth, lower your head, and use your strength evenly." After speaking, I lowered my body to try, and the results were not bad. Although I couldn't help but panic and struggle a bit the first few times, I couldn't swim very far. But after practicing for several afternoons in a row, my hands and feet became proficient. I learned to float, and I also learned to float upside down. And I felt that this kind of floating was more energy-saving, and I could swim across the pond with a diameter of more than ten feet in one breath. It's just that I still couldn't swim. I couldn't stay in the water for more than a minute before I had to rush out to breathe because I felt very suffocated.

Because I had to swim every afternoon, I tied the cow rope to the tree trunk, so that the bull circled around the tree, without the freedom to go far, so as not to eat the vegetables in other people's vegetable gardens or the rice in the fields and cause trouble.

This news spread to my mother's ears a few days later, and my father also knew about it.

"You wild brat, I heard that you've been swimming in the pond for the past few days. It doesn't matter if you drown, but you've made the fat cow thin again. You wild brat!" My father glared at me and scolded me, luckily he didn't hit me.

"I told you not to play in the water, but you lied to me and went. What will you do if you drown! Blind He said you have to be especially careful in July!" My mother only said these two sentences in her kind smile.

The next day, I didn't get up until tea time (Note 8). I knew that the job of herding cows had been transferred to my fourth brother again.

June 10, 1931, in Jiangwan.

(Note 1) is a kind of medicine for stomach pain, (Note 2) means the innate constitution, (Note 3) means invisible, (Note 4) is the local name for pine needles, (Note 5) is a local saying to describe people with no achievements, (Note 6) refers to ordinary family letters, (Note 8) In rural society, there are no clocks, only knowing that it is 9:00 a.m. and 3:00 p.m., saying that it is time to drink tea, so the time is called tea time, and 11:00 a.m. is called wine time. (Note 7) refers to those who work as long-term workers. (The End)

Movie Special

About "Constructive Criticism"

— Ling He

Reading Mr. Liu Huanan's "Respectfully to Movie Critics" on the 16th made me personally feel the importance of my responsibility. Since I am someone who often writes film criticism, I inevitably recognize that I have a close relationship with Chinese films. However, due to my own superficiality, I often feel that I cannot fulfill my duties. Now that Mr. Liu has raised such a significant request, it makes me feel infinitely apprehensive.

Regarding the "constructive criticism" raised by Mr. Liu, I believe that friends who write film criticism should acknowledge the correctness of this issue. In any case, the critic himself is a researcher of film. Therefore, the critic and the author should do their best to seek the progress of Chinese films. At the same time, critics also have the responsibility to faithfully introduce everything about the film to the audience. This is not only to guide the audience on how to appreciate art, but also to make the audience aware of the author's creative intentions. Especially with regard to the former, the audience urgently needs to know the methods or techniques of film creation.

Therefore, in addition to accepting Mr. Liu's suggestion, I have the above-mentioned supplements. The so-called "constructive criticism" not only helps Chinese film authors, but also helps Chinese film audiences. Especially in the current situation where the understanding of the general audience is too weak, everyone engaged in film culture is deeply worried about this. Therefore, constructive criticism has a greater significance in this aspect.

Now, I concretely put forward the following opinions to make this proposal a reality.

The editor of this publication should specially invite a number of experts to, in addition to the general criticism of each new film, also bring up a certain part of a film for everyone to study. For example, everyone admits that the drama component of "Spring Silkworms" is too small. This is of course a failure of the playwright. Then we might as well conduct a detailed exploration of the script. Similarly, we acknowledge that the directors of "慈母恨" or "絕塞情鴻" are very good, and we can also engage in in-depth research. Other aspects such as the makeup of "Wax Museum Mystery," the performance of "Gold Mountain," the set design of "Grand Hotel," or the cinematography and sound recording in other films, are all materials for our research. Of course, we do not have to explore only Chinese films, but the main focus is still on Chinese films. At the same time, we do not have to limit ourselves to existing films. We can even offer opinions to the authors after some research on films that are about to be produced but have not yet started. For example, I think they would be happy to accept our design for the Lianxing Company's adaptation of "Roar, China!" Other things like the "三友式" recorder during the trial period, we can also use this as an opportunity to conduct a study in terms of academic theory.

This is not only of great benefit to film authors, but also readers will definitely feel interested, and the level of appreciation will be improved imperceptibly. Especially since foreign films do not have Chinese versions, there is too much isolation for the audience. If we can translate the dialogues of some films, it would not be a waste of effort. Moreover, introducing the scripts of famous films in general has considerable value.

The above is respectfully offered to the editor of this publication and to those engaged in film culture.

Film Commentary

Review of "龍馬精神" Great Decision

— Ling He

丨Produced by RKO Pictures·Showing in Nanjing丨

This story takes place in the American countryside. The director has fulfilled his responsibility to portray the countryside very well.

The peace of the countryside is surrounded by the smiling faces of everyone in a small shop. Although they are all being harassed by robbers, everyone is still calm and peaceful. However, what is written here is not like "Peach Blossom Spring" in that the countryside is idealized for no reason. What is gratifying is that it truly grasps the simple atmosphere.

There are worldly old people, loyal young people, and affectionate young girls. ... We can see from the scenes where the old man burns the food he is toasting in his hand, the young man buys a piece of bread with all his money, and then receives the box of tobacco from the old man, and the young lovers talk about the milk bottle, etc., that the author is doing his best to show his cleverness.

However, generally speaking, it is still a mediocre work. Although we see the author handling the plot in a fairly delicate way, the grasp of the two climaxes is not strong enough. When the robber forces Tony to become a thief, Tony dies at the hands of the thief, and when his wife and children see the corpse and start crying, we imagine that it must be very tragic, but in fact these few shots fail. This is of course because the actress who plays the mother is too mediocre, and the director cannot remedy it. In addition, although the last climax made the air tense due to the dense gunfire, the old man and the young man were always calm and composed, exaggerating the so-called composure in battle. In this way, the audience feels unreal about the picture.

In this scene, the director is of course responsible for the biggest part, but the two roles playing the old man and the young man did not remedy this shortcoming. Charles Sale, who plays the old man, had excellent results in "生意經". His humorous and lively acting skills make us never forget him. But here we see him trying his best to show the appearance of an old hero, which is not an easy task, so it is not as pleasing to us as "生意經". Bill Boyd has the reputation of "黨人魂", and later also showed a rough and handsome air in "畫舫情痕". But here, there is no special brilliance at all. At best, he is only fulfilling his duties, and he is no different from ordinary mediocre roles.

The mediocre performance is naturally determined by the mediocre story. Here, because the countryside is to be written about being robbed, it is inevitable to create a group of robbers. And this group of robbers are also born evil people. Therefore, it reminds us of the statement in "鐵板紅淚錄" that bandits are produced because of "officials forcing people to rebel," which is indeed pointed out after the author has grasped the economic structure. As for the love interspersed in this work, it is very simple and makes people feel real.

Audience Opinions

My View of "蠻荒之花"

— Yin Zhong

The appearance of foreign "beast films" contains a special and significant meaning. It is used as a propaganda tool for conquering barbaric nations and expanding their colonies. However, the emergence of "beast films" in our country is different in its significance, and there is no significance whatsoever in it. Moreover, the general audience in our country does not understand its significance. They just want to "have fun." Under these circumstances, it goes without saying that foreign beast films are warmly welcomed, and domestic beast films are produced by taking advantage of this point.

However, what exactly is the content and technique of "蛮荒之花," a domestic beast film that has recently been released?

First, let's talk about its content. It is about a pair of unmarried young men and women traveling to Africa, where they encounter terrible beasts and fight with them. Needless to say, this is of course fake. In fact, Chinese people do not even dare to go to their own border areas such as Mongolia, Tibet, and Xinjiang. How dare they run to Africa, a foreign country with poisonous snakes and beasts?

We know that "beast films" are somewhat realistic and journalistic. They are not like other films that can be manufactured artificially. So where does the African background in this film come from? Needless to say, it is copied from foreign films again. Therefore, the completion of this film only relies on the skill of editing. Unfortunately, the editing skill is not very clever, so it is inevitable to reveal flaws, which is the responsibility of the director.

Speaking of performance, the acting skills of the two male and female protagonists are commendable. Compared to the previous film "荒島野人," it is much better. "Omitted below"

My Opinion of "蠻荒之花"

— Shen Gong

The Shanghai film market, which is being occupied by foreign beast films, actually has this "蠻荒之花" domestic beast film. In any case, it is worth taking a breath in terms of competition.

Although beast films are made for the general curious audience, good beast films can also show the difficulty of the filming process and the ability of the technology. For example, films such as "人猿泰山" and "龍虎鬥" can give the audience considerable satisfaction.

They have capital and go to Africa to shoot various strange scenes to use as materials on the screen. We suffer from insufficient capital, so we have to put things together from the East and the West. The value of the concept is not to be discussed, but what is the meaning of the technology? It only shows the clever editing skills!

The themes inevitably have far-fetched parts in order to suit the plot of the film. Is Africa a scenic spot in the world? Why go there for travel? This is completely inexplicable. The barbarian king seems to be as civilized as civilized people and knows about benevolence and righteousness, so he cannot be a barbarian king.

Lions and tigers have long been tired of watching by general curious audiences in many previous foreign films, so they cannot arouse any interest. As for the scene of killing a snake, what is seen in Clara Bow's "野性" Call Her Savage is much more terrifying, but in the "蠻荒之花" film, it is really not easy to support a realistic scene, and it can be regarded as a successful part.

The director's arrangement is relatively lacking in some places and acceptable in others. As for the scenery of Africa, it is originally the skill of other people, so of course it can make people admire it. Among the actors, He Zhigang is the most skilled and can be very competent. Xu Suzhen is also not bad. The other actors can also satisfy people. Especially the performance in several terrifying shots is very realistic.

Tang Xiaodan is a Candidate for the Groom

Li Yun's marriage has sparked talk about marriage in Tianyi Company, and this time Yu Guang, Tang Xiaodan, who were invited to be male bridesmaids, and Lu Lixia and Hu Shan, who were female bridesmaids, have become the center of the discussion. It is said that Yu Guang is already married, and Lu Lixia has long been assigned to Wang Chunyuan. We don't know about Hu Shan. We only know that Lao Tang is still a virgin. Therefore, on the next wedding banquet reservation form, everyone wrote Xiaodan's name. But, who is Lao Tang's target? What day will it be? No one can say for sure. Therefore, Tang Xiaodan has become a candidate for the groom.

Movie Novel Fragrant Grass Beauty (1)

— Tian Fu

Star Film Company Production, Chen Kengran Director, Ma Wenyuan Screenwriter, Actors丨In order of appearance: Xie Yunqing, Xia Peizhen, Wang Zhengxin, Tan Zhiyuan, Gu Lanjun, Xu Xinyuan, Xiao Yingyan, Gong Shang (1) Prologue

It is said that Shanghai is the "den of all evils." The deformed system of society constantly creates many criminals, but then uses something called law to deal with them.

The courthouse is always so lively: batches of criminals are brought in. Then they are interrogated: Why did you commit the crime? Then they ask the "criminal law" doctor to cure the "disease" of crime. Why commit crimes? Let's look at the process of one person's crime! He is one of thousands of criminals: His name is Wang A'da.

(2) Gospel of Life

In the factory of the Da Zhonghua Tobacco Company, there is a large group of people busy making a living there. Clang, clang, clang! They are nailing wooden boxes with all their might: as if their existence is only for nailing wooden boxes.

The tense atmosphere stirred a little, a foreman said: "The company's second branch has been established, and it needs to add more than two thousand male and female workers; if you have relatives and friends, you can introduce them!"

This news spread in everyone's hearts, stirring up a wave of joy. Wang A'da thought of his wife, daughter, and young brother in the countryside, and his heart was moved. So, he registered them with the management office.

Things went so smoothly and luckily, Wang A'da's family's livelihood was easily solved in this way. The wife is in the boxing room, the daughter is in the leaf-picking room, and the brother is pushing and transporting large barrels of tobacco leaves in the warehouse, he has the strength of an ox.

Tall, dark chimneys, coal and fire in the boiler room, the rumbling wheels of the blending room, the knives of the cutting room, the hundreds of anemic hands in the cigarette rolling room... Wang A'da's family lived in such a living environment, but they were very satisfied. Busy during the day, sleeping peacefully at night, sometimes waking up laughing from dreams.

The one-story house, costing a dozen dollars a month, was rented. Although hard work, they were full every day. They lived so peacefully for a year.

(3) Flickering Lamp

Small street, a noisy atmosphere. Small flags with "Please smoke domestic cigarettes, produced by Da Zhonghua Tobacco Company, buy one box get one free" written on them fluttered in the east wind.

The salesman was desperately cranking the hand organ, desperately holding up the loudspeaker and shouting wildly. His mouth was dry from shouting, and people watching the excitement looked at him and left empty-handed.

Small street, a noisy atmosphere. Small flags with "Good tobacco shreds, cheap price, genuinely fair foreign goods" written on them fluttered.

The salesman was desperately cranking the hand organ, desperately holding up the loudspeaker and shouting wildly. His mouth was dry from shouting, and the cigarettes on the cart were almost sold out. (To be continued)

Home
